$$\dots$$
ç”±æ­¤å¾—åˆ°ä¸€ä¸ªé—­åŒºé—´å¥—$\{[a_{n},b_{n}]\}$ï¼Œæ»¡è¶³$a_{n}\notin T,b_{n}\in T,n=1,2,3\dots$
ç”±é—­åŒºé—´å¥—åŸç†ï¼Œå­˜åœ¨å”¯ä¸€å®æ•°$\xi$å±äºæ‰€æœ‰é—­åŒºé—´$[a_{n},b_{n}]$ï¼Œä¸”$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }a_{n}=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }b_{n}=\xi$ï¼Œç°åœ¨åªéœ€è¯´æ˜$\xi$æ˜¯Tçš„æœ€å°æ•°ï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯Sçš„ä¸Šç¡®ç•Œã€‚
è‹¥$\xi \not\in T$ï¼Œå³å®ƒä¸æ˜¯Sçš„ä¸Šç•Œï¼Œåˆ™å­˜åœ¨$x\in S,s.t.\xi<x$ï¼Œç”±$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }b_{n}=\xi$å¯çŸ¥å½“nå……åˆ†å¤§æ—¶ï¼Œæˆç«‹$b_{n}<x$,è¿™ä¸$b_{n}\in T$çŸ›ç›¾ã€‚æ•…$\xi \in T$
è‹¥å­˜åœ¨$\eta \in T,\eta<\xi$ï¼Œç”±$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }a_{n}=\xi$,å¯çŸ¥nå……åˆ†å¤§æ—¶ï¼Œæˆç«‹$\eta<a_{n}$,ç”±äº$a_{n}\not\in T$,äºæ˜¯å­˜åœ¨yï¼Œä½¿å¾—$\eta<a_{n}<y$ï¼Œè¿™ä¸$\eta \in T$çŸ›ç›¾ã€‚ 
è¯æ¯•ã€‚
(3.2)å•è°ƒæœ‰ç•ŒåŸç†
(3.3)Bolzano-Weierstrasså®šç†ï¼šå·²è¯

**(4)Bolzano-Weierstrasså®šç†ä¸ºèµ·ç‚¹ï¼š**
(4.1)ç¡®ç•Œå­˜åœ¨åŸç†
(4.2)å•è°ƒæœ‰ç•ŒåŸç†
(4.3)é—­åŒºé—´å¥—åŸç†
(4.4)Cauchyæ”¶æ•›å‡†åˆ™ï¼šå·²è¯
**(5)Cauchyæ”¶æ•›å‡†åˆ™ä¸ºèµ·ç‚¹ï¼š**
(5.1)ç¡®ç•Œå­˜åœ¨åŸç†
(5.2)å•è°ƒæœ‰ç•ŒåŸç†ï¼š
å‡è®¾å•è°ƒé€’å¢æœ‰ç•Œæ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\}$ä¸æ”¶æ•›
åˆ™ç”±Cauchyæ”¶æ•›å‡†åˆ™æœ‰ï¼š$\exists \varepsilon_{0}>0,\forall N>0,\exists m>n>N:x_{m}-x_{n}<\varepsilon_{0}$
ä»¤$N_{1}=1,\exists m_{1}>m_{0}>N_{1}:x_{m_{1}}-x_{m_{0}}>\varepsilon_{0}$
ä»¤$N_{2}=m_{1},\exists m_{2}>m_{1}=N_{2}:x_{m_{2}}-x_{m_{1}}>\varepsilon_{0}$
$\dots$
ä»¤$N_{k}=m_{k-1},\exists m_{k}>m_{k-1}=N_{k}:x_{m_{k}}-x_{m_{k-1}}>\varepsilon_{0}$
ç´¯åŠ æœ‰$x_{m_{k}}-x_{m_{0}}>k \varepsilon_{0}\to+ \infty(k\to +\infty)$
è¿™ä¸æœ‰ç•Œæ€§çŸ›ç›¾
è¯æ¯•
(5.3)é—­åŒºé—´å¥—åŸç†ï¼š
è®¾$\{[a_{n},b_{n}]\}$æ˜¯ä¸€åˆ—é—­åŒºé—´ï¼Œæ»¡è¶³$[a_{n+1},b_{n+1}]\subset[a_{n},b_{n}],n=1,2,3\dots$ä¸”$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }(b_{n}-a_{n})=0$
è®¾m>nï¼Œåˆ™$0\le a_{m}-a_{n}<b_{n}-a_{n}\rightarrow0(n\rightarrow\infty)$
æ•…$\{a_{n}\}$æ˜¯Cauchyåˆ—ï¼Œä»è€Œ$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }a_{n}=\xi,\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }b_{n}=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }(b_{n}-a_{n})+\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }a_{n}=\xi$
ç”±äº$\{a_{n}\}$å•è°ƒé€’å¢ï¼Œ$\{b_{n}\}$å•è°ƒé€’å‡ï¼Œå¯ä»¥çŸ¥é“$\xi$æ˜¯å±äºæ‰€æœ‰é—­åŒºé—´$[a_{n},b_{n}]$çš„å”¯ä¸€å®æ•°ã€‚
(5.4)Bolzano-Weierstrasså®šç†





# å‡½æ•°æé™ä¸è¿ç»­æ€§
## 1 å‡½æ•°æé™ 
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šå‡½æ•°æé™ã€</span>
>è®¾å‡½æ•°y=f(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$çš„æŸä¸ªå»å¿ƒé‚»åŸŸæœ‰å®šä¹‰ï¼Œå³$\exists \rho>0,s.t.\mathring{U}(x_{0},\rho)\subset D_{f}$.å¦‚æœå­˜åœ¨å®æ•°Aï¼Œå¯¹äº$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists \delta>0,s.t.$å½“$0<|x-x_{0}|<\delta$æ—¶ï¼Œæˆç«‹$|f(x)-A|<\varepsilon$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°Aæ˜¯å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$å¤„çš„æé™ï¼Œè®°ä¸º$\lim\limits_{ x \to x_{0} }f(x)=A$.
>å¦‚æœä¸å­˜åœ¨ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨è¯¥ç‚¹å¤„çš„æé™ä¸å­˜åœ¨ã€‚
>>[!tip]
>>ä¹‹æ‰€ä»¥è¦æ±‚$0<|x-x_{0}|<\delta$ï¼Œè€Œä¸æ˜¯$0\le|x-x_{0}|$ï¼Œæ˜¯å› ä¸ºxåœ¨$x_0$å¤„ä¸ä¸€å®šæœ‰å®šä¹‰ã€‚
>
>==ğŸ–‡ï¸Propertiesï¼š==
>1ï¼‰æé™çš„å”¯ä¸€æ€§ï¼šè®¾Aä¸Bå‡ä¸ºf(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$å¤„çš„æé™ï¼Œåˆ™A=Bã€‚
>2)å±€éƒ¨ä¿åºæ€§ï¼šè‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x\to x_0}f(x)=A,\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }g(x)=B,A>B$ï¼Œä¸”$\exists\delta>0,s.t.$å½“$0<|x-x_{0}|<\delta$æ—¶ï¼Œæˆç«‹$f(x)>g(x)$.
>	Corollary:i.è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=A\ne0,$åˆ™$\exists\delta>0ï¼Œs.t.$å½“$0<|x-x_{0}|<\delta$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$|f(x)|> \frac{|A|}{2}$.
>	ii.è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x\to x_0}f(x)=A,\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }g(x)=B$ï¼Œä¸”$\exists r>0,s.t.$å½“$0<|x-x_{0}|<r$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$g(x)\le f(x)$ï¼Œåˆ™$B\le A$.
>	>[!tip] 
>	>å³ä½¿æ˜¯$g(x)<f(x),$ä¹Ÿ1åªèƒ½å¾—åˆ°$B\le A$çš„ç»“è®ºï¼Œè€Œé$B<A$.
>3)å±€éƒ¨æœ‰ç•Œæ€§ï¼šè‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=A,$åˆ™å­˜åœ¨$\delta>0,s.t.f(x)$åœ¨$\mathring{U}_(x_{0},\delta)$ä¸­æœ‰ç•Œ.
>4)å¤¹é€¼æ€§ï¼šè‹¥$\exists r>0,s.t.$å½“$0<|x-x_{0}|<r$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$g(x)\le f(x)\le h(x),$ä¸”$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }g(x)=\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }h(x)=A$ï¼Œåˆ™$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=A$.
>5ï¼‰å››åˆ™è¿ç®—ï¼šè®¾$\lim_\limits{ x\to x_0}f(x)=A,\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }g(x)=B,$åˆ™ï¼š
>	i.$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }(\alpha f(x)+\beta g(x))=\alpha A+\beta B$
>	ii.$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }(f(x)g(x))=AB$
>	iii.$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{f(x)}{g(x)}=\frac{A}{B}(B \ne0)$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
1)ç±»ä¼¼æ•°åˆ—è¯æ˜ï¼Œåˆ©ç”¨ä¸‰è§’ä¸ç­‰å¼ã€‚
2)å–$\varepsilon=\frac{A-B}{2}$
	i.ç”±äº$||f(x)|-|A||\le|f(x)-A|$å¯çŸ¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }|f(x_{0})|=A$ï¼Œå†å–$g(x)=\frac{|A|}{2}$ï¼Œå³å¯ç”±ä¿åºæ€§è¯æ˜ã€‚
	ii.å‡è®¾B>Aï¼Œç”±ä¿åºæ€§ï¼Œ$\exists\delta>0,s.t.$å½“$0<|x-x_{0}|<\delta$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$g(x)>f(x)$ï¼Œå–$\eta=\min(\delta,r)$ï¼Œåˆ™å½“$0<|x-x_{0}|<\eta$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$g(x)\le f(x)$ï¼ŒçŸ›ç›¾
ä»¥ä¸‹è¯æ˜ç±»ä¼¼æ•°åˆ—è¯æ˜

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
å·²çŸ¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to a}f(x)=A,(a\ge0)$è¯•è¯ï¼š$\lim_\limits{ x \to \sqrt{ a }}f(x^2)=A$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ç”±äº$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta_{1}>0,\forall x(0<|x-a|<\delta_{1}):|f(x)-A|<\varepsilon$
å–$\delta=\min\left( 1, \frac{\delta_{1}}{1+2\sqrt{ a }} \right)$ï¼Œå½“$0<|x-\sqrt{ a }|<\delta$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$0<|x+\sqrt{ a }|<1+2\sqrt{ a }$ï¼Œæ•…$0<|x^2-a|<\delta_{1}$ï¼Œæ•…$|f(x^2)-A|<\varepsilon$
è¯æ¯•

---



> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šå•ä¾§æé™ã€</span>
> 
>è®¾f(x)åœ¨$(x_{0}-\rho,x_{0})(\rho>0)$å¤„æœ‰å®šä¹‰.å¦‚æœ$\exists B \in \mathbb{R}$ï¼Œå¯¹äº$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,s.t.$å½“$-\delta<x-x_{0}<0$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$|f(x_{0})-B|<\varepsilon$,åˆ™ç§°Bæ˜¯å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$å¤„çš„å·¦æé™ï¼Œè®°ä¸º$\lim\limits_{ x \to x_{0^-} }f(x)=f(x_{0^-})=B$.
>å³æé™ç±»ä¼¼ã€‚
>å”¯ä¸€æ€§ï¼Œä¿åºæ€§ï¼Œå››åˆ™è¿ç®—åœ¨å•ä¾§æé™ä¸Šä»ç„¶æˆç«‹ã€‚
>æ˜¾ç„¶ï¼Œå‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$å¤„å­˜åœ¨æé™çš„å……åˆ†å¿…è¦æ¡ä»¶æ˜¯f(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$å¤„çš„å·¦æé™ä¸å³æé™**å­˜åœ¨ä¸”ç›¸ç­‰**ã€‚

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šå¹¿ä¹‰æé™ã€</span>
> 
>å¯¹äºå››ç§å‡½æ•°å€¼å’Œå…­ç§è‡ªå˜é‡å­˜åœ¨æ‰©å……çš„æé™å®šä¹‰ï¼š
>$$\begin{cases}
f(x)\rightarrow A(æœ‰é™):\forall \varepsilon>0,\dots|f(x)-A|<\varepsilon  \\
f(x)\rightarrow \infty:\forall G>0,\dots |f(x)|>G \\
f(x)\rightarrow +\infty:\forall G>0,\dots f(x)>G \\ 
f(x)\rightarrow -\infty:\forall G>0,\dots f(x)<-G 
\end{cases}
\begin{cases}
x \rightarrow x_{0}:\dots,\exists\delta>0,\forall x(0<|x-x_{0}|<\delta):\dots \\
x \rightarrow x_{0^+}:\dots,\exists\delta>0,\forall x(0<x-x_{0}<\delta):\dots \\ 
x \rightarrow x_{0^-}:\dots,\exists\delta>0,\forall x(-\delta<x-x_{0}-\rho<0):\dots  \\
x \rightarrow \infty:\dots,\exists X>0,\forall x(|x|>X):\dots  \\
x \rightarrow +\infty:\dots,\exists X>0,\forall x(x>X):\dots \\
x \rightarrow -\infty:\dots,\exists X>0,\forall x(x<-X):\dots
\end{cases}$$


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
è¯æ˜ï¼šå½“$x\to +\infty$æ—¶,$x^x\gg[x]!\gg a^x\gg x^\alpha\gg \ln^kx\qquad(a>1,\alpha>0,k>0)$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
å…ˆè¯$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty} \frac{[x]!}{x^x}=0$

å†è¯$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty} \frac{a^x}{[x]!}=0$

å†è¯$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty} \frac{x^\alpha}{a^x}=0$
ä»¤$[x]=n,$æœ‰$0<\frac{x^\alpha}{a^x}<\frac{(n+1)^\alpha}{a^n}$
åªéœ€è¯æ˜$\lim_\limits{ n \to +\infty} \frac{n^\alpha}{a^n}=\lim_\limits{ n \to +\infty} \frac{(n+1)^\alpha}{a^n} \frac{n^\alpha}{(n+1)^\alpha}=0$å³å¯
ä»¤æ•°åˆ—$x_{n}=\frac{n^\alpha}{a^n}$,åˆ™$\frac{x_{n+1}}{x_{n}}=\frac{\left( 1+\frac{1}{n} \right)^\alpha}{a}\in\left( \frac{1}{a} , \frac{2^\alpha}{a}\right)$ï¼Œåˆæœ‰$\frac{x_{n+1}}{x_{n}}$é€’å‡ï¼Œ$\frac{1}{a}<1$ï¼Œæ•…ä»æŸé¡¹å¼€å§‹$\frac{x_{n+1}}{x_{n}}<1,$$\{x_{n}\}$é€’å‡ 
å¿½ç•¥å‰æœ‰é™é¡¹ï¼Œæœ‰$\{x_{n}\}$é€’å‡æœ‰ä¸‹ç•Œï¼Œæ•…å…¶æ”¶æ•›ï¼Œè®¾æé™ä»£å…¥$x_{n+1}=x_{n} \frac{a^n}{n^\alpha} \frac{(n+1)^\alpha}{a^{n+1}}$è§£å¾—æé™ä¸º0
æœ€åè¯$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty} \frac{\ln^kx}{x^\alpha}=0$
è®¾$t=\ln x$ï¼Œåˆ™åªéœ€è¯æ˜$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty} \frac{\ln^k x}{x^\alpha}=0$
è¯æ¯•
<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 2 </span>
è¯æ˜**ä¸¤ä¸ªé‡è¦æé™**ï¼š1ï¼‰$\lim_\limits{ x \to \infty}\left( 1+ \frac{1}{x} \right)^x=e$
2ï¼‰$\lim_\limits{ x \to 0} \frac{\sin x}{x}=1$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
1)å…ˆè¯$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty}\left( 1+\frac{1}{x} \right)^x=e$ï¼Œå¯¹äºä»»æ„$x\ge1$ï¼Œæœ‰ï¼š$\left( 1+\frac{1}{[x]+1} \right)^{[x]}<\left( 1+\frac{1}{x} \right)^x<\left( 1+\frac{1}{[x]} \right)^{[x]+1}$
å½“$x\to+\infty$æ—¶ï¼Œä¸ç­‰å¼ä¸¤ä¾§è¡¨ç°ä¸ºä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°åˆ—æé™ï¼Œåˆ©ç”¨å‡½æ•°æé™å¤¹é€¼æ€§å¾—è¯ã€‚
å†è¯$\lim_\limits{ x \to -\infty}\left( 1+\frac{1}{x} \right)^x=e$ï¼Œä»¤$y=-x$ï¼Œäºæ˜¯$x\to +\infty$æ—¶ï¼Œ$y\to -\infty$ï¼Œä»è€Œï¼š
$\lim_\limits{ x \to -\infty}\left( 1+\frac{1}{x} \right)^x=\lim_\limits{ y \to +\infty}\left( 1-\frac{1}{y} \right)^{-y}=\lim_\limits{ y \to +\infty}\left( 1+\frac{1}{y-1} \right)^{y-1}\left( 1+\frac{1}{y-1} \right)=e$
åˆèµ·æ¥ï¼Œå°±å¾—åˆ°ç»“æœ
2ï¼‰

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 3 </span>
è®¡ç®—æé™$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }\prod\limits_{k=1}^n\cos \frac{x}{2^k}$ï¼Œå¹¶è¯æ˜ViÃ¨teå…¬å¼ï¼š$\huge{\frac{\pi}{2}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2} }\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{2}\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2} } }\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2}+\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{2}\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2} } } }\dots}}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$\begin{align}\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }\prod\limits_{k=1}^n\cos \frac{x}{2^k}&=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty } \frac{\cos\frac{x}{2}\cos\frac{x}{2^2}\dots\cos\frac{x}{2^n}\sin\frac{x}{2^n}}{\sin\frac{x}{2^n}}\\&=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty } \frac{\sin x}{2^n\sin\frac{x}{2^n}}\\&=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }\frac{\sin x}{2^n\frac{x}{2^n}}\\&=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty } \frac{\sin x}{x}\end{align}$
ç”±äº$\cos2\theta=-1+2\cos^2\theta$ï¼Œæ•…$\cos \theta=\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{2}\cos2\theta }$
å–$x=\frac{\pi}{2}$å¾—$\cos \frac{x}{2}=\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2} },\cos \frac{x}{4}=\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{ \frac{1}{2} } },\dots$
æ•…$\frac{1}{\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2} }\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{2}\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2} } }\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2}+\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{2}\sqrt{ \frac{1}{2} } } }\dots}=\frac{\frac{\pi}{2}}{\sin \frac{\pi}{2}}=\frac{\pi}{2}$
è¯æ¯•

## 2 å‡½æ•°æé™ä¸æ•°åˆ—æé™
><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:Heineå½’ç»“å®šç†</span>
>  $\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=A$çš„å……åˆ†å¿…è¦æ¡ä»¶æ˜¯ï¼š
>  å¯¹äºä»»æ„æ»¡è¶³æ¡ä»¶$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x_{n}=x_{0}(x_{n}\ne x_{0},n=1,2,3\dots)$çš„æ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\}$ï¼Œç›¸åº”çš„å‡½æ•°å€¼æ•°åˆ—$\{f(x_n)\}$æˆç«‹ï¼š$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x_{n})=A$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$\Longrightarrow:$ ç”±äº$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=A$ï¼Œæœ‰$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,\forall x(0<|x-x_{0}|<\delta):|f(x)-A|<\varepsilon$
ç”±äº$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x_{n}=x_{0},x_{n}\ne x_{0}(n=1,2,3\dots)$ï¼Œå¯¹äºä¸Šè¿°$\delta,\exists N,\forall n>N:0<|x_{n}-x_{0}|<\delta$ 
ç”±æ­¤å½“n>Næ—¶æˆç«‹$|f(x_{n})-A|<\varepsilon$,å³$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x_{n})=A$
$\Longleftarrow:$å‡è®¾f(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$ç‚¹å¤„ä¸ä»¥Aä¸ºæé™ï¼Œå³$\exists \varepsilon_{0}>0,\forall\delta>0,\exists x(0<|x-x_{0}|<\delta):|f(x)-A|\varepsilon_{0}$
ç°å–ä¸€åˆ—$\{\delta_{n}\}= \frac{1}{n}(n=1,2,3\dots)$
å¯¹äº$\delta_{1}=1,\exists x_{1}(0<|x_{1}-x_{0}|<\delta_{1}),s.t.|f(x_{1})-A|\ge\varepsilon_{0};$
å¯¹äº$\delta_{1}= \frac{1}{2},\exists x_{2}(0<|x_{1}-x_{0}|<\delta_{2}),s.t.|f(x_{2})-A|\ge\varepsilon_{0};$
......
ä¸€èˆ¬çš„ï¼Œå¯¹äº$\delta_{k}= \frac{1}{k},\exists x_{k}(0<|x_{k}-x_{0}|<\delta_{k}),s.t.|f(x_{k})-A|\ge\varepsilon_{0};$
äºæ˜¯å¾—åˆ°æ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\}$,æ»¡è¶³$x_{n}\ne x_{0},\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x_{n}=x_{0}$ï¼Œä½†ç›¸åº”çš„å‡½æ•°å€¼æ•°åˆ—$\{f(x_{n})\}$ä¸å¯èƒ½ä»¥Aä¸ºæé™ï¼Œæ•…çŸ›ç›¾ã€‚
è¯æ¯•

> <span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:å¼±Heineå®šç†</span>
> $\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)$å­˜åœ¨çš„å……åˆ†å¿…è¦æ¡ä»¶æ˜¯ï¼š 
> å¯¹äºä»»æ„æ»¡è¶³æ¡ä»¶$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x_{n}=x_{0}(x_{n}\ne x_{0},n=1,2,3\dots)$çš„æ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\}$ï¼Œç›¸åº”çš„å‡½æ•°å€¼æ•°åˆ—$\{f(x_n)\}$æ”¶æ•›

>[!note] 
>å¼±Heineå®šç†æ²¡æœ‰å¼ºè°ƒ$\{f(x_{n})\}$æ˜¯å¦æ”¶æ•›äºåŒä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
åªéœ€è¦æ³¨æ„åˆ°ï¼šè‹¥å­˜åœ¨æ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}'\},\{x_{n}''\},x_{n}'\ne0,x_{n}''\ne0,\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x_{n}'=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x_{n}''=x_{0},ä¸”\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }f(x_{n}')\ne\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }f(x_{n}'')$
å–æ–°çš„æ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\},x_{2n-1}=x_{n}',x_{2n}=x_{n}''$ï¼Œæ˜¾ç„¶$x_{n}\ne x_{0},\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x_{n}=x_{0}$ï¼Œä½†ç›¸åº”çš„å‡½æ•°å€¼æ•°åˆ—å¿…å®šä¸æ”¶æ•›ï¼ŒçŸ›ç›¾ã€‚


> <span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:Cauchyæ”¶æ•›å‡†åˆ™(fun.version)</span>
>  å‡½æ•°æé™$\lim_\limits{ x \to  +\infty }f(x)$å­˜åœ¨ä¸”æœ‰é™çš„å……åˆ†å¿…è¦æ¡ä»¶æ˜¯ï¼š 
>  $\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists X>0,s.t.\forall x',x''>X$ï¼Œæœ‰$|f(x')-f(x'')|<\varepsilon$ 

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$\Longrightarrow:$è®¾$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty }f(x)=A$ï¼ŒæŒ‰ç…§å®šä¹‰ï¼Œ$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists X>0,\forall x',x''>X:|f(x')-A|< \frac{\varepsilon}{2},|f(x'')-A|< \frac{\varepsilon}{2}$ 
äºæ˜¯$|f(x')-f(x'')|\le|f(x')-A|+|f(x'')-A|<\varepsilon$ 
$\Longleftarrow:$ è®¾$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists X>0,\forall x',x''>X:|f(x')-f(x'')|<\varepsilon$
ä»»æ„é€‰å–æ— ç©·å¤§é‡æ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\}$ï¼Œåˆ™å¯¹äºä¸Šè¿°$X>0,\exists N, \forall m>n>N,:x_{n>X}$
æœ‰$|f(x_{m})-f(x_{n})|<\varepsilon$ 
æ•…$\{f(x_{n})\}$æ˜¯Cauchyåˆ—ï¼Œå¿…æ”¶æ•›ã€‚ç”±Heineå½’ç»“å®šç†ï¼Œ$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty}f(x)$å­˜åœ¨ä¸”æ”¶æ•›ã€‚

>[!note] 
>Heineå½’ç»“å®šç†å’ŒCauchyæ”¶æ•›åŸç†å¯¹äºä¸åŒçš„å¹¿ä¹‰æé™å¯ä»¥æœ‰ä¸åŒçš„å½¢å¼ï¼Œä½†å†…å®¹éƒ½æ˜¯ä¸€æ ·çš„ã€‚




## 3 è¿ç»­å‡½æ•°


>  <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šå•ç‚¹è¿ç»­ã€</span>
>  è®¾å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$çš„æŸä¸ª**é‚»åŸŸ**æœ‰å®šä¹‰ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”æˆç«‹$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=f(x_{0})$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°å‡½æ•°åœ¨ç‚¹$x_{0}$å¤„è¿ç»­ï¼Œè€Œç§°$x_{0}$æ˜¯å‡½æ•°f(x)çš„è¿ç»­ç‚¹ã€‚ç”¨ç¬¦å·è¡¨è¿°ä¸ºï¼š$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,\forall x(|x-x_{0}|<\delta):|f(x)-f(x_{0})|<\varepsilon$
>  ç¬¬äºŒå®šä¹‰ï¼š$\lim_\limits{ \Updelta x \to 0}\Updelta y =\lim_\limits{ \Updelta x \to  0 } (f(x+\Updelta x)-f(x))=0$
>
>  >[!caution]
>  >f(x)é¡»åœ¨$x_{0}$å¤„æœ‰å®šä¹‰ã€‚
>
>  >[!tip] 
>  >å‡½æ•°çš„è¿ç»­æ€§å®ç°äº†æé™ä¸å‡½æ•°åçš„æ¢åºï¼Œå³$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=f(\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }x)$
>
>  >[!important] 
>  >è¿ç»­æ€§è¯´çš„å°±æ˜¯åœ¨è¯¥ç‚¹çš„ï¼š**æé™å€¼=å‡½æ•°å€¼**
>
>  å¯¹äºç‚¹$a$çš„é‚»åŸŸ$U(a,\delta)$ï¼Œå®šä¹‰å‡½æ•°$f(x)$åœ¨è¿™ä¸ªé‚»åŸŸä¸Šçš„æŒ¯å¹…ä¸ºï¼š$\omega_{f}(a,\delta)=\sup\limits_{x\in U(a,\delta)}\{ f(x) \}-\inf\limits_{x\in U(a,\delta)}\{ f(x) \}$
>  ç„¶åä»¤$\omega_{f}(a)=\lim_\limits{ \delta \to  0^+ }\omega_{f}(a,\delta)$ç§°ä¸ºå‡½æ•°åœ¨ç‚¹$a$å¤„çš„æŒ¯å¹…
>  å¯¹äºæŒ¯å¹…ï¼Œæ˜“è¯ï¼šå‡½æ•°$f(x)$åœ¨ç‚¹$a$å¤„è¿ç»­çš„å……åˆ†å¿…è¦æ¡ä»¶æ˜¯$\omega_{f}(a)=0$

  
>  <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šå¼€åŒºé—´è¿ç»­ã€</span>
>  è‹¥å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨åŒºé—´(a,b)ä¸Šçš„æ¯ä¸€ç‚¹éƒ½è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨å¼€åŒºé—´(a,b)ä¸Šè¿ç»­ã€‚
>
>  <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šå•ä¾§è¿ç»­ã€</span>
>  è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0^- }f(x)=f(x_{0})$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$å·¦è¿ç»­ã€‚è¡¨è¿°ä¸ºï¼š$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,\forall x(-\delta<x-x_{0}\le \delta):|f(x)-f(x_{0})|<\varepsilon$
>  å³æé™ç±»ä¼¼ã€‚
>  
>>[!note] 
>>ä¸€ä¸ªå‡½æ•°åœ¨è¯¥ç‚¹å·¦è¿ç»­ä¸”å³è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™å‡½æ•°åœ¨è¯¥ç‚¹è¿ç»­ï¼›ä½†åœ¨è¯¥ç‚¹æœ‰å·¦æé™å’Œå³æé™ï¼Œå´ä¸ä¸€å®šæœ‰æé™ã€‚å› ä¸ºæé™è¦æ±‚å·¦å³æé™å­˜åœ¨ä¸”ç›¸ç­‰ï¼Œè€Œè¿ç»­æ€§ç”±äºå·¦å³è¿ç»­éƒ½æ˜¯ä¸è¯¥ç‚¹å‡½æ•°å€¼æ¯”è¾ƒï¼Œå®é™…ä¸Šå·²ç»æš—å«ç›¸ç­‰ã€‚
>
>
>  <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šé—­åŒºé—´è¿ç»­ã€</span>
>  è‹¥f(x)åœ¨(a,b)è¿ç»­ï¼Œä¸”åœ¨å·¦ç«¯ç‚¹aå³è¿ç»­ï¼Œå³ç«¯ç‚¹bå·¦è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨é—­åŒºé—´$[a,b]$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ã€‚
>
>  <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šåŒºé—´è¿ç»­ã€</span>
>  f(x)åœ¨åŒºé—´Iä¸Šæ¯ä¸€ç‚¹éƒ½è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨åŒºé—´Iä¸Šè¿ç»­ã€‚è‹¥IåŒ…å«ç«¯ç‚¹ï¼Œé¡»åœ¨ç«¯ç‚¹å¤„å•ä¾§è¿ç»­ã€‚è¡¨è¿°ä¸ºï¼š$\forall x_{0}\in I,\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,\forall x\in I(|x-x_{0}|< \delta):|f(x)-f(x_{0})|<\varepsilon$

>[!note] 
>ç”¨å®šä¹‰è¯æ˜$f$åœ¨$I$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œé€šå¸¸çš„æ–¹æ³•æ˜¯è®¾æ³•è¯æ˜$f$åœ¨$I$ä¸Šæ»¡è¶³**Lipschitzæ¡ä»¶** ï¼š$|f(x')-f(x'')|\le L|x'-x''|,\forall x',x''\in I$ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­$L>0$æ˜¯æŸä¸€ä¸ªå¸¸æ•°ã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
è¯•è¯æ˜æŒ‡æ•°å‡½æ•°$f(x)=a^x(a>0,a\ne1)$åœ¨$(-\infty,+\infty)$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
å¯¹äºä»»æ„ä¸€ç‚¹$x_{0}\in(-\infty,+\infty)$ï¼Œæœ‰$a^x-a^{x_{0}}=a^{x_{0}}(a^{x-x_{0}}-1)$
æ•…è¦è¯æ˜$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }a^x=a^{x_{0}}$åªéœ€è¯$\lim_\limits{ t \to 0}a^t=1$
$1^\circ$ å½“$t\to0+$æ—¶ï¼Œ
å½“$a>1$æ—¶ï¼Œæˆç«‹$1<a^t\leqslant a^{\frac{1}{\left[ \frac{1}{t} \right]}}$
ç”±äº$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }\sqrt[n]{ a }=1$ï¼Œç”±æé™çš„å¤¹é€¼æ€§ï¼Œ$\lim_\limits{ t \to  0+ }a^t=1$
å½“$0<a<1$æ—¶ï¼Œç”±æé™çš„é™¤æ³•è¿ç®—ï¼Œ$\lim_\limits{ t \to 0+}a^t=\lim_\limits{ t \to 0+} \frac{1}{\left( \frac{1}{a} \right)^t}=\frac{1}{\lim_\limits{ t \to 0+}\left( \frac{1}{a} \right)^t}=1$
$2^\circ$ å½“$t\to0-$æ—¶ï¼Œ
ä»¤$u=-t$ï¼Œåˆ™$\lim_\limits{ t \to 0-}a^t=\lim_\limits{ u \to 0+} \frac{1}{a^u}=1$
åˆèµ·æ¥å°±æœ‰$\lim_\limits{ t \to 0}a^t=1$
è¯æ¯•


---

>  <span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:è¿ç»­å‡½æ•°çš„å››åˆ™è¿ç®—</span>
>è®¾$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=f(x_{0}),\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }g(x)=g(x_{0})$ï¼Œåˆ™ï¼š
>1. $\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }(\alpha f(x)+\beta g(x))=\alpha f(x_{0})+\beta g(x_{0})(\alpha,\betaæ˜¯å¸¸æ•°)$
>2. $\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }(f(x)g(x))=f(x_{0})g(x_{0})$
>3. $\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{f(x)}{g(x)}=\frac{f(x_{0})}{g(x_{0})}(g(x_{0})\ne0)$
>

---

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šä¸è¿ç»­ç‚¹ã€</span>
> å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨ç‚¹$x_{0}$è¿ç»­å¿…é¡»æ»¡è¶³ï¼š

```mermaid
graph
```

>å¦‚æœå‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$ç‚¹ä¸è¿ç»­ï¼Œå³é—´æ–­ï¼Œè€Œ$x_{0}$ç§°ä¸ºf(x)çš„ä¸è¿ç»­ç‚¹æˆ–é—´æ–­ç‚¹ã€‚
> é—´æ–­ç‚¹åˆ†ä¸ºä¸‰ç±»ï¼š
> **ç¬¬ä¸€ç±»**ï¼šå‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨ç‚¹$x_{0}$çš„å·¦å³æé™éƒ½å­˜åœ¨ä½†ä¸ç›¸ç­‰ï¼Œå³$f(x_{0^+})\ne f(x_{0^-})$ã€‚

> >ç¬¬ä¸€ç±»é—´æ–­ç‚¹åˆç§°ä¸ºè·³è·ƒç‚¹ï¼Œå³æé™ä¸å·¦æé™ä¹‹å·®å¯ç§°ä¸ºå‡½æ•°åœ¨è¯¥ç‚¹çš„è·ƒåº¦ã€‚
>
> >[!example] 
> >$f(x)=sgnx,x=0$æ˜¯å®ƒçš„ç¬¬ä¸€ç±»é—´æ–­ç‚¹ï¼Œåœ¨æ­¤å¤„è·ƒåº¦ä¸º2ã€‚
>
> **ç¬¬äºŒç±»**ï¼šå‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨ç‚¹$x_{0}$çš„å·¦å³æé™è‡³å°‘è¦æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªä¸å­˜åœ¨ã€‚
> **ç¬¬ä¸‰ç±»**ï¼šå‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨ç‚¹$x_{0}$çš„å·¦å³æé™å­˜åœ¨ä¸”ç›¸ç­‰ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯ä¸ç­‰äº$f(x_{0})$æˆ–åœ¨ç‚¹$x_{0}$å¤„æ— å®šä¹‰ã€‚
>
> >[!note] 
> >ç”±äºç¬¬ä¸‰ç±»é—´æ–­ç‚¹å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡é‡æ–°å®šä¹‰è¯¥ç‚¹å‡½æ•°å€¼çš„æ–¹å¼ä½¿ä¹‹æˆä¸ºè¿ç»­ç‚¹ï¼Œæ•…ä¹Ÿç§°ä¸ºå¯å»é—´æ–­ç‚¹ã€‚
>
> > [!example]
> >$f(x)=x\sin \frac{1}{x}$ï¼Œå®ƒåœ¨0å¤„æ²¡æœ‰å®šä¹‰ï¼Œä½†å·¦å³æé™éƒ½ç­‰äº0ï¼Œå¯é€šè¿‡é‡æ–°å®šä¹‰ä½¿ä¹‹æˆä¸ºè¿ç»­ç‚¹ã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
Riemannå‡½æ•°çš„å®šä¹‰ä¸ºï¼š
$R(x)=\begin{cases} \frac{1}{p},x= \frac{q}{p},å…¶ä¸­p,qä¸ºäº’ç´ æ•´æ•°ï¼Œp>0ï¼Œq\ne0\\1,x=0\\0,xæ˜¯æ— ç†æ•°\end{cases}$
è¯•è¯æ˜R(x)åœ¨ä»»æ„ç‚¹çš„æé™å­˜åœ¨ä¸”æé™å€¼ä¸º0.æ¢è¨€ä¹‹ï¼Œä¸€åˆ‡æ— ç†ç‚¹æ˜¯å®ƒçš„è¿ç»­ç‚¹ï¼Œä¸€åˆ‡æœ‰ç†ç‚¹æ˜¯å®ƒçš„ç¬¬ä¸‰ç±»é—´æ–­ç‚¹ã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ç”±äºR(x)æ˜¯å‘¨æœŸä¸º1çš„å‘¨æœŸå‡½æ•°ï¼Œæ•…åªéœ€è®¨è®º$[0,1]$åŒºé—´çš„æ€§è´¨ã€‚
ç”±äºå¯¹äºä»»æ„æ­£æ•´æ•°kï¼Œåœ¨$[0,1]$ä¸Šåˆ†æ¯ä¸è¶…è¿‡kçš„æœ‰ç†æ•°ä¸ªæ•°æ˜¯æœ‰é™çš„ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥ï¼š
è®¾$x_{0}\in[0,1]$æ˜¯ä»»æ„ä¸€ç‚¹ï¼Œå¯¹äºä»»æ„ç»™å®šçš„$\varepsilon>0,$è®¾$k= [\frac{1}{\varepsilon}]$ï¼Œè®¾åœ¨$[0,1]$ä¸Šåˆ†æ¯ä¸è¶…è¿‡kçš„æœ‰ç†ç‚¹ä¸º$r_{1},r_{2}\dots r_{n}$,ä»¤$\delta=\min\limits_{1\le i\le n,r_{i}\ne x_{0}}(|r_{i}-x_{0}|)$,æ˜¾ç„¶$\delta>0.$
å½“$x\in[0,1]$ä¸”$0<|x-x_{0}|<\delta$æ—¶ï¼Œè‹¥xæ˜¯æ— ç†æ•°ï¼Œåˆ™$R(x)=0;$è‹¥xæ˜¯æœ‰ç†æ•°ï¼Œå…¶åˆ†æ¯å¿…å®šå¤§äº$\left[  \frac{1}{\varepsilon} \right]$ï¼Œäºæ˜¯$R(x)\le \frac{1}{\left[  \frac{1}{\varepsilon} \right]}+1<\varepsilon$ï¼Œäºæ˜¯æˆç«‹$|R(x)-0|<\varepsilon$ï¼Œæ•…$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }R(x)=0$


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 2 </span>
è¯•è¯æ˜åŒºé—´(a,b)ä¸Šå•è°ƒå‡½æ•°çš„ä¸è¿ç»­ç‚¹å¿…ä¸ºç¬¬ä¸€ç±»ä¸è¿ç»­ç‚¹,ä¸”è‡³å¤šä¸ºå¯æ•°ä¸ªã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ç”±äºå‡½æ•°å•è°ƒä¸”å¤„å¤„æœ‰å®šä¹‰ï¼Œæ•…åªéœ€è¯æ˜å®ƒåœ¨ä»»æ„ç‚¹çš„å·¦å³æé™éƒ½å­˜åœ¨å³å¯ã€‚
ä¸å¦¨è®¾f(x)åœ¨(a,b)ä¸Šå•è°ƒé€’å¢ã€‚
è®¾$x_{0}\in(a,b)$æ˜¯ä»»æ„ä¸€ç‚¹ï¼Œæ˜¾ç„¶é›†åˆ$\{f(x)|x \in(a,x_{0})\}$æœ‰ä¸Šç•Œï¼Œæ•…æœ‰ä¸Šç¡®ç•Œï¼Œè®°å®ƒä¸º$\alpha=\sup\{f(x)|x \in(a,x_{0})\}$
å¯¹äºä¸€åˆ‡$x<x_{0}$ï¼Œæˆç«‹$f(x)\le\alpha$ 
ç”±ç¡®ç•Œå®šä¹‰ï¼Œ$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists x'\in(a,x_{0}),s.t.f(x')>\alpha-\varepsilon$
å–$\delta=x_{0}-x'>0,$åˆ™å½“$-\delta<x-x_{0}<0$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$x'<x<x_{0}$ï¼Œäºæ˜¯æˆç«‹$-\varepsilon<f(x')-\alpha<f(x)-\alpha \le0$
è¿™å°±è¯´æ˜$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0^- }f(x)=\alpha$ï¼ŒåŒæ ·å¯è¯´æ˜$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0^+ }f(x)=\beta,\beta=\inf\{f(x)|x \in(x_{0},b)\}$
>[!tip] 
>å³è¯æ˜$f(x_{0}^-)\le f(x_{0})\le f(x_{0}^+)$
>æ­¤å³ä¸ºå•è°ƒå‡½æ•°çš„å•ä¾§æé™å­˜åœ¨å®šç†

ä¸å¦¨è®¾f(x)ç”±æ— ç©·ä¸ªé—´æ–­ç‚¹ã€‚
è‹¥$x_{0}\in(a,b)$æ˜¯f(x)çš„ä¸€ä¸ªé—´æ–­ç‚¹ï¼Œåˆ™æœ‰$f(x_{0}^-)<f(x_{0}^+)$ï¼Œè¿™æ—¶æœ‰$f(x_{0}^-)\le f(x_{0})\le f(x_{0}^+)$ï¼Œç§°$(f(x^-_{0}),f(x_{0}^+))$ä¸ºé—´æ–­ç‚¹$x_{0}$çš„ä¸€ä¸ªè·³è·ƒåŒºé—´
åªéœ€è¯æ˜ï¼Œä»»æ„ä¸¤ä¸ªä¸åŒçš„é—´æ–­ç‚¹å¯¹åº”çš„è·³è·ƒåŒºé—´ä¸ç›¸äº¤
è®¾$x_{1}$æ˜¯å¦ä¸€ä¸ªé—´æ–­ç‚¹ï¼Œ$x_{1}>x_{0}$
æ’å…¥$x,x'$ï¼Œå³$x_{0}<x<x'<x_{1}$
åˆ™æœ‰$f(x)\le f(x')$
å›ºå®š$x'$ï¼Œä»¤$x\to x_{0}^+$ï¼Œç”±å•è°ƒå‡½æ•°çš„å•ä¾§æé™å­˜åœ¨å®šç†å’Œå‡½æ•°æé™çš„æ¯”è¾ƒå®šç†ï¼Œæœ‰$f(x_{0}^+)\le f(x')$
å†ä»¤$x'\to x_{1}^-$ï¼Œæœ‰$f(x_{0}^+)\le f(x_{1}^-)$ 
äºæ˜¯æœ‰$f(x_{0}^-)\le f(x_{0}^+)\le f(x_{1}^-)\le f(x_{1}^+)$
å³$(f(x^-_{0}),f(x_{0}^+))\cap(f(x^-_{1}),f(x_{1}^+))=\emptyset$
è¯æ¯•

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 3 </span>
ç ”ç©¶å‡½æ•°$f(x)=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty } \frac{x^n-1}{x^n+1}$çš„è¿ç»­æ€§

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Solution ï¼š</span>
æ³¨æ„åˆ°$f(x)=\left\{\begin{align}&1,&|x|>1\\&0,&x=1\\&-1,&|x|<1\\&æ— æ„ä¹‰,&x=-1\end{align}\right.$



---

><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:åå‡½æ•°å­˜åœ¨æ€§å®šç†</span>
>è‹¥å‡½æ•°$y=f(x),x \in D_{f}$æ˜¯ä¸¥æ ¼å•è°ƒå¢åŠ (å‡å°‘)çš„ï¼Œåˆ™å­˜åœ¨å®ƒçš„åå‡½æ•°$x=f^{-1}(y),y\in R_{f}$ï¼Œä¸”$f^{-1}(y)$ä¹Ÿæ˜¯ä¸¥æ ¼å•è°ƒå¢åŠ (å‡å°‘)çš„ã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ä¸å¦¨è®¾$y=f(x),x\in D_{f}$ä¸¥æ ¼å•è°ƒé€’å¢ã€‚
å¯¹äºä»»æ„ä¸¤ç‚¹$x',x''\in D_{f},y'=f(x'),y''=f(x'')$
ç”±é€’å¢å¯çŸ¥$x'<x''\Rightarrow y'<y''$ï¼Œæ˜¾ç„¶å®ƒä¿è¯äº†é€†åƒçš„å”¯ä¸€æ€§ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥å­˜åœ¨åå‡½æ•°$x=f^{-1}(y),y\in R_{f}$


> <span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:åå‡½æ•°è¿ç»­æ€§å®šç†</span>
> è®¾å‡½æ•°$y=f(x)$åœ¨é—­åŒºé—´$[a,b]$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ä¸”ä¸¥æ ¼å•è°ƒå¢åŠ ï¼Œ$f(a)=\alpha,f(b)=\beta$ï¼Œåˆ™å®ƒçš„åå‡½æ•°$x=f^{-1}(y)$åœ¨$[\alpha,\beta]$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ä¸”ä¸¥æ ¼å•è°ƒå¢åŠ ã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
é¦–å…ˆè¯æ˜$[\alpha,\beta]$ä¸Šçš„ä»»æ„ä¸€ç‚¹éƒ½æœ‰åŸåƒ,å³$f([a,b])=[\alpha,\beta]$:
æ˜¾ç„¶$[\alpha,\beta]\in f([a,b])$.è®¾$\gamma\in(\alpha,\beta)$æ˜¯ä»»æ„ä¸€ç‚¹ï¼Œè®°$S=\{x|x\in(a,b),f(x)<\gamma\}$ï¼ŒSéç©ºæœ‰ä¸Šç•Œæ•…å¿…æœ‰ä¸Šç¡®ç•Œï¼Œè®°$x_{0}=\sup S,x_{0}\in(a,b)$
ç”±äºf(x)ä¸¥æ ¼å•è°ƒé€’å¢ï¼Œå½“$x<x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$f(x)<\gamma$;å½“$x>x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$f(x)>\gamma$,ç”±ä¸Šè¿°eg.2,æœ‰$f(x_{0^-})\le\gamma\le f(x_{0^+})$
ç”±äºf(x)åœ¨$x_{0}$è¿ç»­ï¼Œå¾—åˆ°$f(x_{0})=f(x_{0^-})=f(x_{0^+})=\gamma$,è¿™å°±è¯´æ˜$f(x)$çš„å€¼åŸŸæ˜¯$[\alpha,\beta]$ï¼Œåˆç”±äºåå‡½æ•°å­˜åœ¨æ€§å®šç†ï¼Œ$f^{-1}(y)$ä¸¥æ ¼å•è°ƒé€’å¢

ç°åœ¨åªéœ€è¦è¯æ˜åå‡½æ•°$x=f^{-1}(y)$åœ¨$[\alpha,\beta]$ä¸Šçš„è¿ç»­æ€§
è®¾$y_{0}\in(\alpha,\beta)$ï¼Œç›¸åº”çš„æœ‰$f^{-1}(y_{0})=x_{0}\in(a,b)$
$\forall \varepsilon>0,$ä»¤$y_{1}=f(x_{0}-\varepsilon),y_{2}=f(x_{0}+\varepsilon)$ï¼Œå–$\delta=\min(y_{0}-y_{1},y_{2}-y_{0})$ï¼Œæ˜¾ç„¶å½“$|y-y_{0}|<\delta$æ—¶ï¼Œæˆç«‹$|f^{-1}(y)-f^{-1}(y_{0})|<\varepsilon$
å¦‚æœ$y_{0}=\alpha$ï¼Œåªéœ€è¯æ˜å³è¿ç»­æ€§ï¼›å¦‚æœ$y_{0}=\beta$ï¼Œåªéœ€è¯æ˜å·¦è¿ç»­æ€§ï¼›
è¯æ¯•

---

><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:å¤åˆå‡½æ•°è¿ç»­æ€§å®šç†</span>
>è‹¥$u=g(x)$åœ¨ç‚¹$x_{0}$å¤„è¿ç»­ï¼Œ$g(x_{0})=u_{0}$ï¼Œåˆæœ‰$y=f(u)$åœ¨$u_{0}$è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™å¤åˆå‡½æ•°$y=f\circ g(x)$åœ¨ç‚¹$x_{0}$è¿ç»­ã€‚ 

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists \eta>0,\forall u(|u-u_{0}|<\eta):|f(u)-f(u_{0})|<\varepsilon$
å¯¹äºä¸Šè¿°$\eta>0,$ç”±äº$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }g(x)=g(x_{0})=u_{0}$ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥$\exists\delta>0,\forall x(|x-x_{0}|<\delta):|g(x)-u_{0}|<\eta$
å› æ­¤ï¼Œå½“$|x-x_{0}|<\delta$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰$|f\circ g(x)-f\circ g(x_{0})|<\varepsilon$ 
è¯æ¯•

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
è¯•è¯æ˜å¯¹äºä»»ä½•å®æ•°$\alpha$ï¼Œå¹‚å‡½æ•°$f(x)=x^\alpha$åœ¨$(0,+\infty)$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ã€‚

è®¾f,gæ˜¯$(-\infty,+\infty)$ä¸Šçš„è¿ç»­å‡½æ•°ï¼Œåˆåœ¨æ‰€æœ‰æœ‰ç†ç‚¹ä¸Šæœ‰$f(x)=g(x)$ï¼Œè¯•è¯æ˜$f(x)\equiv g(x)$

åªéœ€è¯æ˜$\mathbb{R}$ä¸­æ¯ä¸ªæ— ç†ç‚¹xæœ‰$f(x)=g(x)$å³å¯

$1^\circ:$ ç”±äºé›†åˆ$\{fçš„æ­£å‘¨æœŸ\}$æœ‰ä¸‹ç•Œ0ï¼Œç”±ç¡®ç•Œå­˜åœ¨å®šç†ï¼Œ$\inf\{fçš„æ­£å‘¨æœŸ\}=T_{0}$å­˜åœ¨

## 4 æ— ç©·å¤§é‡ä¸æ— ç©·å°é‡ 
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šæ— ç©·å°é‡ã€</span>
> è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=0,$åˆ™ç§°å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶f(x)æ˜¯æ— ç©·å°é‡ï¼Œç”¨$o(1)$è¡¨ç¤ºã€‚
> >[!note] 
> >æ— ç©·å°é‡æ˜¯ä»¥0ä¸ºæé™çš„å˜é‡ï¼Œ$x\rightarrow x_{0}$å¯ä»¥æ‰©å……è‡³å…¶ä»–æƒ…å†µã€‚

><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>æ— ç©·å°é‡çš„æ¯”è¾ƒ</span>
>è®¾$u(x),v(x)$æ˜¯ä¸¤ä¸ªå˜é‡ï¼Œå½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œå®ƒä»¬éƒ½æ˜¯æ— ç©·å°é‡ï¼Œæ¯”è¾ƒ$\frac{u(x)}{v(x)}$çš„æé™æƒ…å†µï¼š
>
>**1)** è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{u(x)}{v(x)}=0$ï¼Œè¡¨ç¤ºå½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œu(x)è¶‹äº0çš„é€Ÿåº¦æ¯”v(x)å¿«ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬ç§°ï¼š
>å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œu(x)å…³äºv(x)æ˜¯é«˜é˜¶æ— ç©·å°é‡ï¼Œæˆ–v(x)å…³äºu(x)æ˜¯ä½é˜¶æ— ç©·å°é‡ï¼Œè®°ä¸ºï¼š
>$u(x)=o(v(x))\quad(x\rightarrow x_{0})$
>>[!Help] 
>>äº‹å®ä¸Šï¼Œ$u(x)=o(v(x))\quad(x\rightarrow x_{0})$ä»£è¡¨çš„æ„æ€æ˜¯$u(x)\in o(v(x)),0(v(x))$å¯ä»¥çœ‹ä½œæ¯”$v(x)$é«˜é˜¶çš„æ— ç©·å°é‡å‡½æ•°çš„é›†åˆã€‚å› æ­¤ï¼Œä¸èƒ½å†™ä½œ$o(v(x))=u(x)$
>
>
>**2)** è‹¥å­˜åœ¨A>0ï¼Œå½“xåœ¨$x_{0}$çš„æŸä¸ªå»å¿ƒé‚»åŸŸä¸­ï¼Œæˆç«‹ï¼š$| \frac{u(x)}{v(x)}|\le A$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°ï¼š
>å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œ$\frac{u(x)}{v(x)}$æ˜¯æœ‰ç•Œé‡ï¼Œè®°ä¸ºï¼š
>$u(x)=O(v(x))\quad(x\rightarrow x_{0})$
>è‹¥åˆå­˜åœ¨a>0,å½“xåœ¨$x_{0}$çš„æŸä¸ªå»å¿ƒé‚»åŸŸä¸­ï¼Œæˆç«‹ï¼š$a\le| \frac{u(x)}{v(x)}|\le A$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°ï¼š
>å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶,u(x)ä¸v(x)æ˜¯åŒé˜¶æ— ç©·å°é‡ã€‚
>æ˜¾ç„¶ï¼Œè‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }\frac{u(x)}{v(x)}=c\ne0$ï¼Œåˆ™u(x)ä¸v(x)å¿…æ˜¯åŒé˜¶æ— ç©·å°é‡ã€‚
>
>**3)** è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{u(x)}{v(x)}=1$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°ï¼š
>å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶,u(x)ä¸v(x)æ˜¯ç­‰ä»·æ— ç©·å°é‡ã€‚è®°ä¸ºï¼š
>$u(x)\sim v(x)\quad(x\rightarrow x_{0})$
>ä¸Šå¼ä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥å†™æˆï¼š$u(x)=v(x)+o(v(x))\quad(x\rightarrow x_{0})$
>

>[!important] 
>==æ— ç©·å°é‡çš„è¿ç®—æ³•åˆ™==ï¼š
> $x\rightarrow0$æ¡ä»¶ä¸‹ï¼Œå¯¹äº$m>0,n>0$ï¼Œæœ‰ï¼š
>**åŠ æ³•å¸æ”¶æ€§ï¼š** $o(x^m)\pm o(x^n)=o(x^{\min(m,n)})$
>**ä¹˜æ³•ç´¯ç§¯æ€§ï¼š** $x^mo(x^n)=o(x^{m+n})\qquad o(x^m)o(x^n)=o(x^{m+n})$
>**å¸¸æ•°ä¸åŠ¨æ€§ï¼š** $ko(x^n)=o(x^n)\qquad o(kx^n)=o(x^n)(k\ne0,kå¯æ›¿æ¢æˆä»»æ„æœ‰ç•Œå‡½æ•°)$
>**å¤åˆæ€§ï¼š** $o(x+o(x))=o(x)\qquad o(o(x))=o(x)$
>


>[!important] 
>==å¸¸è§ç­‰ä»·æ— ç©·å°é‡==ï¼š
> å½“$x\rightarrow0$æ—¶,
>$$\begin{matrix} \sin x\sim x&\tan x\sim x &\arcsin x\sim x &\arctan x\sim x \\
>1-\cos x\sim \frac{1}{2}x^2&\tan x-x\sim \frac{1}{3}x^3&x-\sin x\sim \frac{1}{6}x^3&\tan x-\sin x\sim \frac{1}{2}x^3 \\
>\arcsin x-x\sim \frac{1}{6}x^3&x-\arctan x\sim \frac{1}{3}x^3 \\ \\
>e^x-1\sim x&a^x-1\sim x\ln a \\
>\ln(1+x)\sim x&\log_{a}(1+x)\sim \frac{x}{\ln a} \\ \\
>(1+x)^\alpha-1\sim\alpha x \\  \\
>x-\ln(1+x)\sim \frac{1}{2}x^2 \\ \\
>\ln(x+\sqrt{ 1+x^2 })\sim x\end{matrix}$$
>
>å½“$x\rightarrow\infty$æ—¶ï¼š
>$\lim_\limits{ x \to \infty}\left( 1+ \frac{1}{x} \right)^x\sim e$
>
>å…¶ä¸­çš„$x$ä»£è¡¨çš„å…¶å®æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªåœ¨å¯¹åº”ç‚¹è¶‹äº0æˆ–$\infty$çš„å‡½æ•°ã€‚





---

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šæ— ç©·å¤§é‡ã€</span>
> è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)=\infty(æˆ–\pm \infty),$åˆ™ç§°å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶f(x)æ˜¯æ— ç©·å¤§é‡ã€‚


><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>æ— ç©·å¤§é‡çš„æ¯”è¾ƒ</span>
>è®¾$u(x),v(x)$æ˜¯ä¸¤ä¸ªå˜é‡ï¼Œå½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œå®ƒä»¬éƒ½æ˜¯æ— ç©·å¤§é‡ï¼Œæ¯”è¾ƒ$\frac{u(x)}{v(x)}$çš„æé™æƒ…å†µï¼š
>
>**1)** è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{u(x)}{v(x)}=\infty$ï¼Œè¡¨ç¤ºå½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œu(x)è¶‹äºæ— ç©·å¤§çš„é€Ÿåº¦æ¯”v(x)å¿«ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬ç§°ï¼š
>å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œu(x)å…³äºv(x)æ˜¯é«˜é˜¶æ— ç©·å¤§é‡ï¼Œæˆ–v(x)å…³äºu(x)æ˜¯ä½é˜¶æ— ç©·å¤§é‡
>
>**2)** è‹¥å­˜åœ¨A>0ï¼Œå½“xåœ¨$x_{0}$çš„æŸä¸ªå»å¿ƒé‚»åŸŸä¸­ï¼Œæˆç«‹ï¼š$| \frac{u(x)}{v(x)}|\le A$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°ï¼š
>å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶ï¼Œ$\frac{u(x)}{v(x)}$æ˜¯æœ‰ç•Œé‡ï¼Œè®°ä¸ºï¼š
>$u(x)=O(v(x))\quad(x\rightarrow x_{0})$
>è‹¥åˆå­˜åœ¨a>0,å½“xåœ¨$x_{0}$çš„æŸä¸ªå»å¿ƒé‚»åŸŸä¸­ï¼Œæˆç«‹ï¼š$a\le| \frac{u(x)}{v(x)}|\le A$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°ï¼š
>å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶,u(x)ä¸v(x)æ˜¯åŒé˜¶æ— ç©·å¤§é‡ã€‚
>æ˜¾ç„¶ï¼Œè‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }\frac{u(x)}{v(x)}=c\ne0$ï¼Œåˆ™u(x)ä¸v(x)å¿…æ˜¯åŒé˜¶æ— ç©·å¤§é‡ã€‚
>
>**3)** è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{u(x)}{v(x)}=1$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°ï¼š
>å½“$x\rightarrow x_{0}$æ—¶,u(x)ä¸v(x)æ˜¯ç­‰ä»·æ— ç©·å¤§é‡ã€‚è®°ä¸ºï¼š
>$u(x)\sim v(x)\quad(x\rightarrow x_{0})$


><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:ç­‰ä»·é‡æ›¿æ¢åŸç†</span>
>**ä¹˜ç§¯æ›¿æ¢ï¼š** è®¾$\alpha(x),\beta(x),\beta'(x)$åœ¨$x_{0}$çš„æŸä¸ªå»å¿ƒé‚»åŸŸæœ‰å®šä¹‰ï¼Œä¸”$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{\beta(x)}{\beta'(x)}=1$ï¼Œå³$\beta(x)\sim \beta'(x)(x\rightarrow x_{0})$ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆï¼š
>1ï¼‰å½“$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }\alpha(x)\beta(x)=A$æ—¶ï¼Œ$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }\alpha(x)\beta'(x)=A$
>2ï¼‰å½“$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{\alpha(x)}{\beta(x)}=A$æ—¶ï¼Œ$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{\alpha(x)}{\beta'(x)}=A$
>**å’Œå·®æ›¿æ¢ï¼š** è®¾$\alpha(x),\alpha'(x),\beta(x),\beta'(x)$åœ¨$x_{0}$çš„æŸä¸ªå»å¿ƒé‚»åŸŸæœ‰å®šä¹‰ï¼Œä¸”$\alpha(x)\sim\alpha'(x),\beta(x)\sim\beta'(x)(x\rightarrow x_{0}),\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{\alpha'(x)}{\beta'(x)}=c(c\ne1)$ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆï¼š
>å½“$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }(\alpha(x)-\beta(x))=A$æ—¶ï¼Œ$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }(\alpha'(x)-\beta'(x))=A$
>å®šç†çš„è¯æ˜å¯ä»¥ç”±æé™çš„å››åˆ™è¿ç®—æ³•åˆ™ç›´æ¥å¾—åˆ°ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­$x\rightarrow x_{0}$å¯ä»¥æ›¿æ¢ä¸ºå…¶ä»–çš„æé™æƒ…å†µã€‚


>[!caution] 
>ä½¿ç”¨ç­‰ä»·æ— ç©·å°é‡æ›¿æ¢éœ€è¦æ³¨æ„ä»¥ä¸‹å‡ ç‚¹ï¼š
>1ï¼‰è¢«æ›¿æ¢çš„é‡ï¼Œå¿…é¡»æ˜¯æ— ç©·å°é‡ï¼ˆåœ¨å–æé™æ—¶ä¸º0ï¼‰ã€‚
>2ï¼‰**æ›¿æ¢æ—¶å¿…é¡»æ•´ä½“æ›¿æ¢ï¼Œè€Œä¸èƒ½æ›¿æ¢å±€éƒ¨ã€‚** ä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯è¯´æˆ‘ä»¬æ±‚$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)\pm g(x)$Â æ—¶ï¼Œå¦‚æœÂ f(x)Â å’ŒÂ g(x)Â éƒ½æœ‰æé™ï¼Œé‚£æ— æ‰€è°“ï¼Œå› ä¸ºå¯ä»¥æ‹†æˆä¸¤ä¸ªæé™åˆ†åˆ«æ±‚ç»“æœï¼Œç„¶ååœ¨åŠ èµ·æ¥ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥ç›¸å½“äºç‹¬ç«‹æ±‚ä¸¤ä¸ªçš„æé™ï¼Œä½†å¦‚æœåªæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªæœ‰æé™ï¼Œæˆ–ä¸¤ä¸ªéƒ½æ²¡æœ‰ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨ç­‰ä»·æ— ç©·å°é‡çš„æ›¿æ¢æ—¶ï¼Œå°±å¿…é¡»è¦æ•´ä½“æ›¿æ¢ã€‚

>[!tip] 
>ç­‰ä»·æ— ç©·å°é‡çš„æ›¿æ¢æœ¬è´¨ä¸Šå°±æ˜¯ä½¿ç”¨Taylorå…¬å¼çš„ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹å»ä¼°è®¡æé™å€¼ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥ï¼Œç­‰ä»·ä»£æ¢å¯ä»¥è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜ï¼ŒTaylorå…¬å¼ä¹Ÿä¸€å®šå¯ä»¥ï¼Œä½†åè¿‡æ¥å°±ä¸ä¸€å®šäº†ã€‚
>åŠ å‡ä¸èƒ½éšæ„æ›¿æ¢çš„åŸå› æ˜¯åŠ å‡å¯èƒ½ä¼šå¯¼è‡´é¡¹çš„æŠµæ¶ˆï¼ŒæŠµæ¶ˆåï¼Œæ ¹æ®åˆ†æ¯çš„é˜¶æ•°å¯èƒ½ä¼šéœ€è¦æ³°å‹’å±•å¼€ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹åçš„é«˜é˜¶è¿‘ä¼¼ï¼Œä½†å› ä¸ºç­‰ä»·æ— ç©·å°é‡åªå–äº†æ³°å‹’å±•å¼€çš„ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹ï¼Œå¯¹åç»­çš„è¿‘ä¼¼æ— èƒ½ä¸ºåŠ›ã€‚
>ä½†æ˜¯ä¹˜é™¤å¯ä»¥éšæ„ä½¿ç”¨æ›¿æ¢ï¼Œå› ä¸ºä¹˜é™¤ä¸ä¼šæ¶ˆå»ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹è¿‘ä¼¼ï¼Œç­‰ä»·çš„é‚£ä¸ªæ— ç©·å°é‡ï¼ˆå³æ³°å‹’å±•å¼€çš„ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹ï¼‰æ€»ä¼šåœ¨ï¼Œåœ¨å°±æ„å‘³ç€è½®ä¸åˆ°åé¢çš„é«˜é˜¶è¿‘ä¼¼ä¸Šåœºã€‚
>å› æ­¤ï¼Œåªè¦è®©ç›¸åŠ å‡çš„ä¸¤ä¸ªå‡½æ•°çš„æ³°å‹’å±•å¼€å¼çš„ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹ï¼ˆç­‰ä»·çš„æ— ç©·å°é‡ï¼‰ä¸ä¼šè¢«æ¶ˆå»å°±å¯ä»¥åœ¨åŠ å‡æ—¶ä½¿ç”¨æ›¿æ¢ï¼Œå¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š
>å·²çŸ¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{\alpha(x)}{\beta(x)}$å­˜åœ¨ï¼Œ$\alpha(x),\alpha'(x),\beta(x),\beta'(x)$éƒ½æ˜¯$x\rightarrow x_{0}$çš„æ— ç©·å°é‡ï¼Œä¸”$\alpha(x)\sim\alpha'(x),\beta(x)\sim\beta'(x)$ï¼š
>è‹¥$\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 } \frac{\alpha(x)}{\beta(x)}\ne1$(ä¸¤è€…Taylorå±•å¼€ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹ä¸ç›¸åŒ)ï¼Œåˆ™$\alpha-\beta\sim\alpha'-\beta'$

>[!note] 
>å°†ä¸è¶…è¿‡xçš„ç´ æ•°ä¸ªæ•°è®°ä¸º$\pi(x)$ï¼Œåˆ™æœ‰ç´ æ•°å®šç†ï¼š$\pi(x)\sim \frac{x}{\ln x}(x\to+\infty)$



## 5 é—­åŒºé—´ä¸Šçš„è¿ç»­å‡½æ•°
>[!tip] 
>çº¦å®šè®°å·$C_{[a,b]}=\{f(x)|f(x)åœ¨[a,b]ä¸Šè¿ç»­\}$(continuous)

><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:æœ‰ç•Œæ€§å®šç†</span>
>è‹¥å‡½æ•°$f(x)\in C_{[a,b]},$åˆ™å®ƒåœ¨$[a,b]$ä¸Šæœ‰ç•Œã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
å‡è®¾$f(x)$åœ¨ $[a,b]$ä¸Šæ— ç•Œã€‚
å°† $[a,b]$ç­‰åˆ†ä¸ºä¸¤ä»½ï¼Œåˆ™è¿™ä¸¤ä¸ªåŒºé—´è‡³å°‘æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªæ— ç•Œï¼Œé€‰å‡ºå…¶ä¸­æ— ç•Œçš„ï¼Œä¾æ¬¡è¿›è¡Œä¸‹å»ï¼Œå¾—åˆ°é—­åŒºé—´å¥— $\{[a_{n},b_{n}]\}$ï¼Œä¸” $f(x)$åœ¨å…¶ä¸­ä»»ä½•ä¸€ä¸ª$[a_{n},b_{n}]$éƒ½æ˜¯æ— ç•Œçš„ã€‚
æ ¹æ®é—­åŒºé—´å¥—åŸç†ï¼Œå­˜åœ¨å”¯ä¸€å®æ•°$\xi$å±äºæ‰€æœ‰$[a_{n},b_{n}]$ä¸”ï¼š$\xi=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }a_{n}=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }b_{n}$
åˆæœ‰$f(x)$åœ¨$\xi$ç‚¹è¿ç»­ï¼Œæ•…è€Œ$\exists\delta>0,M>0,\forall x\in U(\xi,\delta)\cap[a,b]$æˆç«‹$|f(x)|\le M$
å¯¹äºå……åˆ†å¤§çš„nï¼Œåˆæœ‰$[a_{n},b_{n}]\subset U(\xi,\delta)\cap[a,b]$,æ•…$f(x)$åœ¨è¿™äº›$[a_{n},b_{n}]$ä¸Šæœ‰ç•Œï¼ŒçŸ›ç›¾ã€‚
è¯æ¯•

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof 2ï¼ˆBolzano-Weierstrassï¼‰ï¼š</span>
å‡è®¾$f(x)$åœ¨$[a,b]$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ä½†æ— ç•Œ
ç”±äºæ— ç•Œè¡¨è¿°ä¸ºï¼š$\forall G>0,\exists x\in[a,b],s.t.|f(x)|>G$
å–$G_{n}=n$ï¼Œå¾—åˆ°ç‚¹åˆ—$\{ x_{n} \}$æ»¡è¶³$|f(x_{n})|>n$ï¼Œå³$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }f(x_{n})=\infty$
ç”±Bolzano-Weierstrasså®šç†ï¼Œå­˜åœ¨å­åˆ—$\{ x_{n_{k}} \},\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }x_{n_{k}}=\xi,\xi\in[a,b]$
ç”±äº$f(x)$åœ¨$\xi$è¿ç»­ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥$\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }f(x_{n_{k}})=f(\xi)$
è¿™ä¸$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }f(x_{n})=\infty$çŸ›ç›¾
è¯æ¯•

><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:æœ€å€¼å®šç†</span>
>è‹¥å‡½æ•°$f(x)\in C_{[a,b]},$åˆ™å®ƒåœ¨$[a,b]$ä¸Šä¸€å®šèƒ½å–åˆ°æœ€å¤§å€¼å’Œæœ€å°å€¼ï¼Œå³å­˜åœ¨$\xi,\eta\in[a,b],s.t.\forall x\in[a,b]:f(\xi)\le f(x)\le f(\eta).$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ç”±äºæœ‰ç•Œæ€§ï¼Œé›†åˆ$R_{f}=\{f(x)|x\in[a,b]\}$æœ‰ç•Œï¼Œæ•…å¿…æœ‰ä¸Šä¸‹ç¡®ç•Œï¼Œè®¾$\alpha=\sup R_{f},\beta=\inf R_{f}$
åªéœ€è¯æ˜å­˜åœ¨$\xi\in[a,b],s.t.f(\xi)=\alpha,\beta$åŒç†ã€‚
ç”±äº$\forall x\in[a,b],$æœ‰$f(x)\le \alpha$ï¼›$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists x\in[a,b],s.t.f(x)>\alpha-\varepsilon$ 
å–$\varepsilon_{n}=\frac{1}{n}$ï¼Œå¾—åˆ°æ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\},x_{n}\in[a,b],$æ»¡è¶³$\alpha-\frac{1}{n}<f(x_{n})\le \alpha$
ç”±Bolzano-Weierstrasså®šç†ï¼Œå¯¹äºæ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\}$å­˜åœ¨æ”¶æ•›å­åˆ—$\{x_{n_{k}}\}$ï¼Œ$\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }x_{n_{k}}=\xi,\xi\in[a,b]$
åˆæœ‰$f(x)$åœ¨$\xi$ç‚¹è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆæœ‰æé™çš„å¤¹é€¼æ€§ï¼Œæ•…$f(\xi)=\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }f(x_{n_{k}})=f(\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }x_{n_{k}})=\alpha$
è¯æ¯•


><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:é›¶ç‚¹å­˜åœ¨å®šç†</span>
>è‹¥å‡½æ•°$f(x)\in C_{[a,b]},$ä¸”$f(a)f(b)<0,$åˆ™ä¸€å®šå­˜åœ¨$\xi\in(a,b),s.t.f(\xi)=0.$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ä¸å¦¨è®¾$f(a)<0,f(b)>0,$å®šä¹‰é›†åˆ$V=\{x|f(x)<0,x\in[a,b]\},$æ˜¾ç„¶Væœ‰ä¸Šç•Œæ•…å¿…æœ‰ä¸Šç¡®ç•Œ$\xi=\sup V$
ç°è¯æ˜$\xi\in(a,b)$ä¸”å®ƒæ˜¯$f(x)$çš„ä¸€ä¸ªé›¶ç‚¹ã€‚
ç”±æé™çš„ä¿åºæ€§ï¼Œ$\exists \delta_{1}>0,\forall x\in[a,a+\delta_{1}]:f(x)<0;\exists \delta_{2}>0,\forall x\in[b-\delta_{2},b]:f(x)>0$.
äºæ˜¯$a+\delta_{1}\le \xi\le b-\delta_{2},$å³è¯$\xi\in(a,b)$
å–$\{x_{n}\}\in V(n=1,2,3\dots),\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x_{n}=\xi,$ç”±äº$f(x_{n})<0,$æœ‰$f(\xi)=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }f(x_{n})\le0$
å‡è®¾$f(\xi)<0,$ç”±$f(x)$åœ¨$\xi$çš„è¿ç»­æ€§ï¼Œ$\exists\delta>0,\forall x\in U(\xi,\delta):f(x)<0,$è¿™ä¸$\xi=\sup V$çŸ›ç›¾ï¼Œäºæ˜¯å¿…ç„¶æœ‰$f(\xi)=0$
è¯æ¯•

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof 2 ï¼š</span>
è®¾$a=a_{1},b=b_{1}$
å¦‚æœ$f\left( \frac{a_{1}+b_{1}}{2} \right)=0$ï¼Œåˆ™å®šç†å¾—è¯ï¼›å¦‚æœ$f\left( \frac{a_{1}+b_{1}}{2} \right)<0$ï¼Œåˆ™ä»¤$a_{2}=\frac{a_{1}+b_{1}}{2},b_{2}=b_{1}$ï¼›å¦‚æœ$f\left( \frac{a_{1}+b_{1}}{2} \right)>0$ï¼Œåˆ™ä»¤$a_{2}=a_{1},b_{2}=\frac{a_{1}+b_{1}}{2}$ï¼›
å¦‚æœ$f\left( \frac{a_{2}+b_{2}}{2} \right)=0$ï¼Œåˆ™å®šç†å¾—è¯ï¼›å¦‚æœ$f\left( \frac{a_{2}+b_{2}}{2} \right)<0$ï¼Œåˆ™ä»¤$a_{3}=\frac{a_{2}+b_{2}}{2},b_{3}=b_{2}$ï¼›å¦‚æœ$f\left( \frac{a_{2}+b_{2}}{2} \right)>0$ï¼Œåˆ™ä»¤$a_{3}=a_{2},b_{3}=\frac{a_{2}+b_{2}}{2}$ï¼›
$\dots$
ä»¥æ­¤ç±»æ¨ï¼Œå¦‚æœå­˜åœ¨æŸä¸ªkï¼Œä½¿å¾—$f\left( \frac{a_{k}+b_{k}}{2} \right)=0$ï¼Œåˆ™å®šç†å¾—è¯ï¼›å¦‚æœä¸å­˜åœ¨ï¼Œåˆ™å¾—åˆ°ä¸€ä¸ªé—­åŒºé—´å¥—$\{ [a_{n},b_{n}] \}$ï¼Œæ»¡è¶³$f(a_{n})<0,f(b_{n})>0$
ç”±é—­åŒºé—´å¥—åŸç†ï¼Œå¯çŸ¥å­˜åœ¨$\xi\in[a_{n},b_{n}],\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }a_{n}=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }b_{n}=\xi$
ç”±$f(x)$åœ¨$\xi$çš„è¿ç»­æ€§ï¼Œå¯çŸ¥$f(\xi)=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }a_{n}\leqslant0,f(\xi)=\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }b_{n}\geqslant0$
ä»è€Œ$f(\xi)=0$
è¯æ¯•


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
è‹¥å‡½æ•°$f(x)\in C_{[a,b]},$ä¸”$f([a,b])\subset[a,b]$ï¼Œåˆ™å­˜åœ¨$\xi\in[a,b],s.t.f(\xi)=\xi,$è¿™æ ·çš„$\xi$ç§°ä¸ºf(x)çš„ä¸€ä¸ª**ä¸åŠ¨ç‚¹**ã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
å³è¯$g(x)=f(x)-x$å­˜åœ¨é›¶ç‚¹ã€‚
ç”±äº$f([a,b])\subset[a,b],$æ•…æœ‰$g(a)\le0,g(b)\ge0$
è‹¥$g(a)=0æˆ–g(b)=0$é›¶ç‚¹å­˜åœ¨æ€§å·²è¯ï¼›è‹¥å¦ï¼Œç”±é›¶ç‚¹å­˜åœ¨å®šç†ï¼Œå¾—è¯ã€‚
è¯æ¯•

><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:ä»‹å€¼å®šç†</span>
>è‹¥å‡½æ•°$f(x)\in C_{[a,b]},$åˆ™å®ƒä¸€å®šèƒ½å–åˆ°æœ€å¤§å€¼$M=\max\{f(x)|x\in[a,b]\}$å’Œæœ€å°å€¼$m=\max\{f(x)|x\in[a,b]\}$ä¹‹é—´çš„ä»»ä½•ä¸€ä¸ªå€¼ã€‚

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ç”±æœ€å€¼å®šç†ï¼Œ$\exists \xi,\eta\in[a,b],s.t.f(\xi)=m,f(\eta)=M,$ä¸å¦¨è®¾$\xi<\eta,$å¯¹äºä»»æ„ä¸€ä¸ªä¸­é—´å€¼$C,m<C<M,$ä»¤$\varphi(x)=f(x)-C$
ç”±äº$\varphi(x)$åœ¨é—­åŒºé—´$[a,b]$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ï¼Œ$\varphi(\xi)<0,\varphi(\eta)>0,$ç”±é›¶ç‚¹å­˜åœ¨å®šç†$\exists \zeta\in(\xi,\eta),s.t.\varphi(\zeta)=0,å³f(x)=C$

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­æ€§ã€</span>
> è®¾å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨åŒºé—´Iä¸Šå®šä¹‰ï¼Œè‹¥$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,\forall x',x''\in I(|x'-x''|<\delta):|f(x')-f(x'')|<\varepsilon$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨åŒºé—´Iä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ã€‚
> æ˜¾ç„¶ï¼Œf(x)åœ¨åŒºé—´Iä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­$\Longrightarrow$f(x)åœ¨åŒºé—´$I$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ï¼Œä½†é€†å‘½é¢˜ä¸ä¸€å®šæˆç«‹ã€‚

>[!note] 
>è¿ç»­æ€§çš„$\delta$ä¾èµ–äº$\varepsilon,x_{0}$;ä½†ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­æ€§çš„$\delta$åªä¾èµ–äº$\varepsilon$ï¼Œå³å¯¹äºæ‰€æœ‰$x_{0}$éƒ½æˆç«‹ã€‚
>ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­æ€§åæ˜ åˆ°å›¾åƒä¸Šè¡¨ç°ä¸ºæ¯”è¾ƒå¹³ç¼“ã€‚



><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­æ€§å®šç†</span>
>è®¾å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨åŒºé—´Iä¸Šå®šä¹‰ï¼Œåˆ™f(x)åœ¨Iä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­çš„å……è¦æ¡ä»¶æ˜¯ï¼š
>å¯¹äºä»»æ„ç‚¹åˆ—$\{x'_{n}\},\{x''_{n}\}(x'_{n},x''_{n}\in I)$ï¼Œåªè¦æ»¡è¶³$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }(x'_{n}-x''_{n})=0,$å°±æœ‰$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }(f(x'_{n})-f(x''_{n}))=0$. 

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$\Longrightarrow:$ ç”±äºä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œæœ‰$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,\forall x',x''\in I(|x'-x''|<\delta):|f(x')-f(x'')|<\varepsilon$
å¯¹äºä»»æ„ç‚¹åˆ—$\{x'_{n}\},\{x''_{n}\}(x'_{n},x''_{n}\in I)$ï¼Œç”±äºæ»¡è¶³$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }(x'_{n}-x''_{n})=0,$æ•…å¯¹äºä¸Šè¿°$\delta$ï¼Œ$\exists N,\forall n>N:|x'_{n}-x''_{n}|<\delta,$å› è€Œæœ‰$|f(x'_{n})-f(x''_{n})|<\varepsilon$,å³è¯$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }(f(x'_{n})-f(x''_{n}))=0$
$\Longleftarrow:$ å‡è®¾f(x)åœ¨Iä¸Šä¸ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™ï¼š$\exists \varepsilon>0,\forall\delta>0,\exists x',x''\in I(|x'-x''|<\delta):|f(x')-f(x'')|\ge \varepsilon$
å–$\delta_{n}=\frac{1}{n},$å¾—åˆ°æ•°åˆ—$\{x'_{n}\},\{x''_{n}\}(x'_{n},x''_{n}\in I),$æ»¡è¶³$|x'_{n}-x''_{n}|< \frac{1}{n},|f(x')-f(x'')|\ge \varepsilon$
æ˜¾ç„¶ï¼Œ$\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }(x'_{n}-x''_{n})=0,ä½†|f(x')-f(x'')|$ä¸å¯èƒ½æ”¶æ•›äº0.
è¯æ¯•

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šLipschitzæ¡ä»¶ã€</span>
> è‹¥$\exists L>0,s.t.\forall x_{1},x_{2}\in I:|f(x_{1})-f(x_{2})|<L|x_{1}-x_{2}|$ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°å‡½æ•°$f(x)$åœ¨åŒºé—´Iä¸Šæ»¡è¶³Lipschitzæ¡ä»¶ï¼›è‹¥$L<1$ï¼Œfç§°ä¸ºæ”¶ç¼©æ˜ å°„
> åŒºé—´Iä¸Šæ»¡è¶³Lipschitzæ¡ä»¶çš„å‡½æ•°ä¸€å®šæ˜¯ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­çš„

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$\forall \varepsilon>0,å–\delta=\frac{\varepsilon}{L}å³å¯$
è¯æ¯•

><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:Cantorå®šç†</span>
>è‹¥å‡½æ•°$f(x)\in C_{[a,b]},$åˆ™å®ƒåœ¨åŒºé—´$[a,b]$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ã€‚ 

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
å‡è®¾f(x)åœ¨Iä¸Šä¸ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™ï¼š$\exists \varepsilon>0,\forall\delta>0,\exists x',x''\in I(|x'-x''|<\delta):|f(x')-f(x'')|\ge \varepsilon$
å–$\delta_{n}=\frac{1}{n},$å¾—åˆ°æ•°åˆ—$\{x'_{n}\},\{x''_{n}\}(x'_{n},x''_{n}\in I),$æ»¡è¶³$|x'_{n}-x''_{n}|< \frac{1}{n},|f(x')-f(x'')|\ge \varepsilon$ 
ç”±äº$\{x'_{n}\}$æœ‰ç•Œï¼Œæ•…å­˜åœ¨æ”¶æ•›å­åˆ—$\{x'_{n_{k}}\},\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x'_{n_{k}}=\xi,\xi\in[a,b].$
å–$\{x''_{n}\}$çš„å­åˆ—$\{x''_{n_{k}}\}$,å…¶ä¸‹æ ‡ä¸$\{x'_{n_{k}}\}$ç›¸åŒï¼Œåˆ™ç”±$|x'_{n_{k}}-x''_{n_{k}}|< \frac{1}{n_{k}}$ï¼Œæœ‰$\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }x''_{n}=\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }(x'_{n}+x''_{n}-x'_{n})=\xi$
åˆæœ‰å‡½æ•°$f(x)$åœ¨$\xi$è¿ç»­,æœ‰$\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }f(x'_{n})=\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }f(x''_{n})=f(\xi)$
äºæ˜¯$\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }(f(x'_{n})-f(x''_{n}))=0$ï¼Œè¿™ä¸$|f(x')-f(x'')|\ge \varepsilon$çŸ›ç›¾
è¯æ¯•

><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Corollary</span>
>å‡½æ•°f(x)åœ¨æœ‰é™å¼€åŒºé—´$(a,b)$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™å®ƒåœ¨$(a,b)$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­çš„å……è¦æ¡ä»¶æ˜¯ï¼š$f(a+),f(b-)$å­˜åœ¨ã€‚


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$\Longleftarrow:$å®šä¹‰å‡½æ•°$g(x)=\begin{cases}f(a+),x=a\\f(x),a<x<b\\f(b-),x=b\end{cases}$
åˆ™å‡½æ•°$g(x)$æ˜¯é—­åŒºé—´$[a,b]$ä¸Šçš„ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­å‡½æ•°ï¼Œå®šä¹‰åŸŸç¼©å°æ—¶ï¼Œä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­æ€§ä»ç„¶æˆç«‹ã€‚
$\Longleftarrow:$ $\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,\forall x',x''\in(a,b)(|x'-x''|<\delta):f(x')-f(x'')<\varepsilon$ 
åœ¨åŒºé—´$(a,b)$ä¸Šä»»æ„é€‰å–æ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\},x_{n}\in(a,b),\lim_\limits{ n \to \infty }x_{n}=a$
ç”±äº$\{x_{n}\}$æ˜¯Cauchyåˆ—ï¼Œä»è€Œå¯¹äºä¸Šè¿°$\delta,\exists N,\forall n,m>N:|x_{n}-x_{m}|<\delta$ ï¼Œå› æ­¤$|f(x_{n})-f(x_{m})|<\varepsilon$ 
ç”±Heineå½’ç»“å®šç†ï¼Œ$f(a+)=\lim_\limits{ x \to a+}f(x)$å­˜åœ¨ã€‚ $f(b-)$ç›¸ä»¿è¯æ˜
è¯æ¯•

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
$f(x)\in C_{[a,+\infty]},\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty}f(x)=A(æœ‰é™)$ï¼Œè¯•è¯ï¼š$f(x)$åœ¨$[a,+\infty)$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ 

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ç”±Cauchyæ”¶æ•›å‡†åˆ™ï¼Œ$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists X>0,\forall x',x''>X(x',x''\in[a,+\infty)):|f(x')-f(x'')|<\varepsilon$
ç”±äº$f(x)$åœ¨$[a,X+1]$ä¸Šè¿ç»­ï¼Œå› æ­¤å¿…å®šåœ¨$[a,X+1]$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œå³ï¼š
$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta_{0}>0,\forall x_{1},x_{2}\in[a,X+1](|x_{2}-x_{1}|<\delta_{0}):|f(x_{1})-f(x_{2})|<\varepsilon$ 
è®¾$\delta=\min(\delta_{0},1)$ï¼Œåˆ™å¯¹äº$\forall x_{1},x_{2}$ï¼Œå½“$|x_{1}-x_{2}|<\delta$æ—¶ï¼Œæœ‰ä¸‰ç§æƒ…å½¢ï¼š
(1)$x_{1},x_{2}\in[X,+\infty)$ï¼Œåˆ™ç”±ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªä¸ç­‰å¼å¾—ï¼š$|f(x_{1})-f(x_{2})|<\varepsilon$ 
(2)$x_{1}\in[X,+\infty),x_{2}\in[a,X]$(æˆ–äº’æ¢)ï¼Œç”±$|x_{1}-x_{2}|<\delta\leqslant1$çŸ¥ï¼š
$x_{1}\in[a,X+1],x_{2}\in[a,X+1]$
å› æ­¤$|f(x_{1})-f(x_{2})|<\varepsilon$ 
(3)$x_{1},x_{2}\in[a,X]$ï¼Œç”±é—­åŒºé—´ä¸Šè¿ç»­å¾—ï¼š$|f(x_{1})-f(x_{2})|<\varepsilon$
ç»¼ä¸Šæ‰€è¿°ï¼Œ$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,\forall|x_{1}-x_{2}|<\delta:|f(x_{1})-f(x_{2})|<\varepsilon$ 
å³$f(x)$åœ¨$[a,+\infty)$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ 
è¯æ¯•


>[!warning] 
>é”™è¯¯è¯æ˜ï¼š
>$1^\circ$ç”±Cauchyæ”¶æ•›å‡†åˆ™ï¼Œ$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists X>0,\forall x',x''>X(x',x''\in[a,+\infty)):|f(x')-f(x'')|<\varepsilon$ï¼Œç”±äº$\varepsilon$çš„ä»»æ„æ€§ï¼Œ$f(x)$åœ¨$[X,+\infty]$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œ
>$2^\circ$å†ç”±Cantorå®šç†ï¼Œ$f(x)$åœ¨$[a,M+1]$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œ
>$3^\circ$æ‰€ä»¥$f(x)$åœ¨$[a,+\infty)$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­
>é”™è¯¯ä¹‹å¤„åœ¨äº$1^\circ$ä¸­çš„$X$ä¸$\varepsilon$æœ‰å…³ï¼Œç”±äº$\varepsilon$çš„ä»»æ„æ€§ï¼Œ$X$åº”è¯¥æ˜¯åŠ¨æ€çš„ï¼Œç”±$1^\circ$å¾—ä¸å‡º$f(x)$åœ¨$[X,+\infty]$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­
>

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 2 </span>
åˆ©ç”¨ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­çš„å®šä¹‰è¯æ˜ï¼šè‹¥$f(x)$åœ¨$(a,b)$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™$f(x)$åœ¨ä¸Šé¢æœ‰ç•Œ

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ç”±äº$f(x)$åœ¨$(a,b)$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œå–$\varepsilon=1,\exists\delta>0,\forall |x_{1}-x_{2}|<\delta(x_{1},x_{2}\in(a,b)):|f(x_{1})-f(x_{2})|<1$
å–$n\in \mathbb{N}^+,s.t. \frac{b-a}{n}<\delta$ï¼Œå°†$(a,b)$nç­‰åˆ†ï¼Œè®°åˆ†ç‚¹$x_{k}=a+\frac{k}{n}(b-a),\quad(k=0,1,\dots n)$
$\forall x,\exists0\leqslant k\leqslant n-1,s.t.x_{k}\leqslant x\leqslant x_{k+1}$
åˆ™$|x-\frac{x_{k}+x_{k+1}}{2}|\leqslant x_{k+1}-x_{k}<\delta$
åˆ™$|f(x)|\leqslant|f(x)-f\left( \frac{x_{k}+x_{k+1}}{2} \right)|+|f\left( \frac{x_{k}+x_{k+1}}{2} \right)|\leqslant1+\max\limits_{0\leqslant k\leqslant n-1}|f\left( \frac{x_{k}+x_{k+1}}{2} \right)|$
è¯æ¯•

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 3 </span>
$f(x)\in C_{[0,+\infty)},f(x)\in D_{(0,+\infty)},\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty }|f'(x)|=A$ï¼Œè¯•è¯æ˜å½“ä¸”ä»…å½“Aæœ‰é™æ—¶ï¼Œ$f(x)$åœ¨$[0,+\infty)$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$1^\circ$ å½“Aæœ‰é™æ—¶ï¼Œç”±äº$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty }|f'(x)|=A$ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥$\exists N>0,\forall x>N:|f'(x)|<A+1$
ç”±Lagrangeä¸­å€¼å®šç†ï¼Œ$\forall x_{1},x_{2}>N,(x_{1}>x_{2}),\exists \xi\in(x_{2},x_{1}):f(x_{1})-f(x_{2})=f'(\xi)(x_{1}-x_{2})$
å› æ­¤ï¼Œ$|f(x_{1})-f(x_{2})|<(A+1)|x_{1}-x_{2}|$æ»¡è¶³Lipschitzæ¡ä»¶ï¼Œå› è€Œåœ¨$[N,+\infty)$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´æ”¶æ•›
åœ¨$[0,N]$ä¸Šï¼Œç”±Cantorå®šç†ï¼Œä¸€è‡´æ”¶æ•›ï¼›åˆèµ·æ¥å°±æœ‰ï¼Œ$f(x)$åœ¨$[0,+\infty)$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´æ”¶æ•›

$2^\circ$ å½“Aæ— é™æ—¶ï¼Œ
ç”±äº$\lim_\limits{ x \to +\infty}|f'(x)|=+\infty$ï¼Œæ•…$\forall G>0,\exists X>0,\forall x>X:|f'(x)|>G$
$\exists \varepsilon_{0}=1,\forall\delta>0,\exists x'=2X,x''=2X+\frac{1}{G}$ï¼Œæ˜¾ç„¶åªè¦Gè¶³å¤Ÿå¤§å°±æœ‰$|x'-x''|<\delta$
ç”±Lagrangeä¸­å€¼å®šç†ï¼Œ$|f(x')-f(x'')|=|f'(\xi)||x'-x''|>G\cdot \frac{1}{G}=1=\varepsilon_{0}$
æ•…$f(x)$åœ¨$[0,+\infty)$éä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­
è¯æ¯•

>[!note] 
>è¿™æä¾›äº†ä¸€ç§åˆ¤æ–­ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­çš„ç®€ä¾¿æ–¹æ³•
>äº‹å®ä¸Šï¼Œå¯æ”¹ä¸º$f(x)\in D_{I},\exists M>0,s.t.|f'(x)|\leqslant M$ï¼Œæœ‰ï¼Œ$f(x)$åœ¨$I$ä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œå³å¯¼å‡½æ•°æœ‰ç•Œå³å¯

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 4 </span>
è¯•è¯æ˜ï¼šè¿ç»­å‘¨æœŸå‡½æ•°å¿…ç„¶ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
è®¾$f(x)$æœ‰å‘¨æœŸTï¼Œå°†$\mathbb{R}$åˆ†æˆå‘¨æœŸæ®µï¼š$I_{i}=[iT,(i+1)T](i\in \mathbb{Z})$
ç”±Cantorå®šç†ï¼Œåœ¨$[-T,2T]$ä¸Šï¼Œ$\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta_{1}>0,\forall|x'-x''|<\delta_{1}:|f(x')-f(x'')|<\varepsilon$
å–$d=\min\{ \delta_{1},T \}$å³å¯
è¯æ¯•

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 5 </span>
Iä¸ºæœ‰é™åŒºé—´ï¼Œfåœ¨Iä¸Šæœ‰å®šä¹‰ï¼Œè¯•è¯ï¼š$f(x)$åœ¨Iä¸Šä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­çš„å……è¦æ¡ä»¶æ˜¯ï¼šfæŠŠCauchyåºåˆ—æ˜ å°„æˆCauchyåºåˆ—

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$\Longrightarrow:$ $\forall \varepsilon>0,\exists\delta>0,\forall |x'-x''|<\delta(x',x''\in I):|f(x')-f(x'')|<\varepsilon$
è®¾$\{ x_{n} \}$ä¸ºCauchyåºåˆ—ï¼Œåˆ™å¯¹äºè¯¥$\delta>0,\exists N>0,\forall m,n>0,|x_{m}-x_{n}|<\delta$ï¼Œä»è€Œ$|f(x_{m})-f(x_{n})|<\varepsilon$
$\Longleftarrow:$ å‡è®¾$f(x)$åœ¨Iä¸Šä¸ä¸€è‡´è¿ç»­ï¼Œåˆ™$\exists \varepsilon_{0}>0,\forall\delta_{n}=\frac{1}{n}>0,\exists|x_{n}-x'_{n}|<\delta(x_{n},x'_{n}\in I):|f(x_{n})-f(x'_{n})|\geqslant\varepsilon_{0}$
ç”±äºIä¸ºæœ‰é™åŒºé—´ï¼Œç”±Bolzano-Weierstrasså®šç†å­˜åœ¨æ”¶æ•›å­åˆ—$\{ x_{n_{k}} \},\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }x_{n_{k}}=\eta$
å–$\{ x'_{n} \}$ä¸­ä¸‹æ ‡ç›¸åŒçš„å­åˆ—ï¼Œç”±$|x_{n}-x'_{n}|\to0(n\to \infty)$ï¼Œå› æ­¤$\lim_\limits{ k \to \infty }x'_{n_{k}}=\eta$
ä½œæ•°åˆ—$x_{n_{1}},x'_{n_{1}},x_{n_{2}},x'_{n_{2}},\dots x_{n_{k}},x'_{n_{k}}$ï¼Œæ˜¾ç„¶å®ƒæ”¶æ•›ï¼Œä¸ºCauchyåºåˆ—
è€Œå¯¹äºå¯¹åº”çš„å‡½æ•°å€¼æ•°åˆ—ï¼Œæœ‰$|f(x_{n_{k}})-f(x'_{n_{k}})|\geqslant\varepsilon_{0}$ä¸æ˜¯Cauchyæ•°åˆ—ï¼ŒçŸ›ç›¾
è¯æ¯•

>[!note] 
>Içš„æœ‰é™æ€§åªåœ¨å……åˆ†æ€§æ—¶ç”¨åˆ°ã€‚å¯¹äºæ— ç©·åŒºé—´ï¼Œå¿…è¦æ€§ä»ç„¶æˆç«‹

## 6 å‘¨æœŸä¸‰è•´å«æ··æ²Œ
â€”â€”Period 3 implies chaos

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šä¸€ç»´è¿­ä»£åŠ¨åŠ›ç³»ç»Ÿã€</span>
> é€’æ¨å…¬å¼$x_{n+1}=f(x_{n}),n\in \mathbb{N}_{+}$ï¼Œåœ¨åŠ¨åŠ›ç³»ç»Ÿç†è®ºä¸­ç§°ä¸ºä¸€ç»´è¿­ä»£åŠ¨åŠ›ç³»ç»Ÿï¼ˆæˆ–ä¸€ç»´ç¦»æ•£åŠ¨åŠ›ç³»ç»Ÿï¼‰
> ä»åˆå€¼$x_{0}$å‡ºå‘ç”±è¿­ä»£ç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªæ•°åˆ—$\{x_{n}\}_{n\ge0}$ï¼Œç§°ä¸ºç”±åˆå€¼$x_{0}$ç¡®å®šçš„**è½¨é“**ã€‚
> å¦‚æœå¯¹äºæŸä¸€è½¨é“$\{x_{n}\}$å­˜åœ¨æ­£æ•´æ•°ï¼Œä½¿$x_{n+p}=x_{n}$å¯¹äºä»»æ„$n\ge0$æˆç«‹ï¼Œåˆ™ç§°è¯¥è½¨é“æ˜¯ä»¥pä¸ºå‘¨æœŸçš„å‘¨æœŸè½¨ï¼Œå‘¨æœŸè½¨ä¸­çš„ç‚¹ç§°ä¸ºå‘¨æœŸç‚¹ã€‚
> å¯¹äºå‘¨æœŸè½¨æ¥è¯´ï¼Œå…·æœ‰ä»¥ä¸Šæ€§è´¨çš„æœ€å°pç§°ä¸ºè½¨çš„æœ€å°å‘¨æœŸã€‚

>è®¾fæ˜¯åœ¨æœ‰ç•Œé—­åŒºé—´$I_{0},I_{1}\dots I_{n-1}$ä¸Šæœ‰å®šä¹‰çš„è¿ç»­å‡½æ•°ï¼Œæ»¡è¶³$f(I_{0})\supset I_{1}f(I_{1})\supset I_{2}\dots f(I_{n-2})\supset I_{n-1},f(I_{n-1})\supset I_{0}$
>åˆ™å­˜åœ¨ç‚¹$x_{0}$,ä½¿å¾—$f^n(x_{0})=x_{0}$ï¼Œä¸”$f^i(x_{0})\in I_{i},i=1,2,3\dots n-1$
><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:Li-Yorkeç¬¬ä¸€å®šç†</span>
>è®¾Iä¸ºåŒºé—´ï¼Œå‡½æ•°$f\in C(I)$ï¼Œä¸”æœ‰$f(I)\subset I$,è®¾æœ‰ç‚¹a,b,c,då±äºåŒºé—´Iï¼Œæ»¡è¶³$f(a)=b,f(b)=c,f(c)=d,\quad d\le a<b<c(æˆ–d\ge a>b>c)$ï¼Œåˆ™fæœ‰æœ€å°æ­£å‘¨æœŸä¸ºæ¯ä¸ªæ­£æ•´æ•°çš„æ‰€æœ‰å‘¨æœŸè½¨ã€‚


>[!note] 
>è®°å¤åˆå‡½æ•°$f(f(x))$ä¸º$f^2(x)$ï¼Œä¸€èˆ¬çš„,è®°ï¼š
>$f^n(x)=\underbrace{f(f(\dots f(x)\dots))}_{né‡}$


><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:Li-Yorkeç¬¬äºŒå®šç†</span>
>è®¾Iä¸ºåŒºé—´ï¼Œå‡½æ•°$f\in C(I)$ï¼Œä¸”æœ‰$f(I)\subset I$,åˆ™åœ¨åŒºé—´Iä¸­å­˜åœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªä¸å¯åˆ—é›†Sï¼Œä½¿å¾—ä»¥Sä¸­ä»»ä½•ä¸¤ç‚¹$x,y(x\ne y)$ä¸ºåˆå€¼çš„è¿­ä»£ç”Ÿæˆæ•°åˆ—$\{f^n(x)\},\{f^n(y)\}$å…·æœ‰ä»¥ä¸‹æ€§è´¨ï¼š
>$1^\circ \varlimsup\limits_{ n \to \infty }|f^n(x)-f^n(y)|>0$
>$2^\circ \varliminf\limits_{ n \to \infty }|f^n(x)-f^n(y)|=0$
>$3^\circ \varlimsup\limits_{ n \to \infty }|f^n(x)-f^n(p)|>0$(pæ˜¯fçš„ä»»æ„ä¸€ä¸ªå‘¨æœŸç‚¹)


> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:æ–¹æ­£é¾™çˆªç®€ä½“;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>ã€ŒDefinitionï¼šLi-Yorkeæ··æ²Œã€</span>
> è®¾fåœ¨åŒºé—´Iä¸Šæœ‰å®šä¹‰ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”$f(I)\subset I.$å¦‚æœæ»¡è¶³ä»¥ä¸‹æ¡ä»¶ï¼š
> (1)fçš„å‘¨æœŸç‚¹çš„æœ€å°å‘¨æœŸæ— ä¸Šç•Œ
> (2)å­˜åœ¨Içš„ä¸å¯åˆ—å­é›†Sï¼Œå¯¹äºSä¸­ä»»æ„ä¸¤ç‚¹$x,y(x\ne y)$ï¼Œå‡æœ‰ï¼š

## 7 å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹
><span style='font-family:æ±‰ä»ªåŠ²æ¥·ç®€ Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem</span>
>ä¸€æ¬¡é½æ¬¡å‡½æ•°$f(x)=ax$æ»¡è¶³å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹$f(x+y)=f(x)+f(y)\quad(\forall x,y\in \mathbb{R})$ 
>å‡½æ•°$f(x)=a^x(a>0)$æ»¡è¶³å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹$f(x+y)=f(x)\cdot f(y)\quad(\forall x,y\in \mathbb{R})$ 
>å‡½æ•°$f(x)=\log_{a}x(a>0)$æ»¡è¶³å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹$f(xy)=f(x)+f(y)\quad(\forall x,y>0)$ 
>å‡½æ•°$f(x)=x^a$æ»¡è¶³å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹$f(xy)=f(x)\cdot f(y)\quad(\forall x,y>0)$ 
>å‡½æ•°$f(x)=\cos ax,g(x)=\mathrm{ch}\,ax$æ»¡è¶³å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹$f(x+y)+f(x-y)=2f(x)\cdot f(y)\quad(\forall x,y\in \mathbb{R})$ 
>å‡½æ•°$f(x)=\sin ax$ä¸$g(x)=\cos ax$æ»¡è¶³å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹ç»„$\begin{cases}f(x+y)=f(x)f(y)-g(x)g(y)\\g(x+y)=f(x)g(y)+f(y)g(x)\end{cases}$ 


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹$f(x+y)=f(x)+f(y)\quad(\forall x,y\in \mathbb{R})$åœ¨$x=0$å¤„è¿ç»­çš„å”¯ä¸€è§£æ˜¯$f(x)=ax$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$1^\circ$ å…ˆè¯æ˜$\forall c\in(-\infty,+\infty):f(cx)=cf(x)$
$1.1^\circ$ å…ˆè¯æ˜$\forall n\in \mathbb{N}:f(nx)=nf(x)$
å½“$n=2$æ—¶ï¼Œ$f(2x)=f(x+x)=f(x)+f(x)$æˆç«‹
å‡è®¾n-1æ—¶ä»æˆç«‹å³$f[(n-1)x]=(n-1)f(x)$
å¯¹äºnï¼Œæœ‰$f(nx)=f[(n-1)x+x]=(n-1)f(x)+f(x)=nf(x)$
ç”±å½’çº³æ³•åŸç†$\forall n\in \mathbb{N}:f(nx)=nf(x)$
$1.2^\circ$ å†è¯æ˜$\forall r\in \mathbb{Q^+}:f(rx)=rf(x)$
ä»¤$y=nx$ï¼Œåˆ™$f(y)=nf\left( \frac{y}{n} \right)$ï¼Œå³$f\left( \frac{1}{n}y \right)=\frac{1}{n}f(y)$
ç”±äº$\forall n\in \mathbb{N}:f(nx)=nf(x)$ï¼Œæœ‰$f\left( \frac{m}{n}y \right)=\frac{m}{n}f(y)\quad(\forall m,n\in \mathbb{N})$
ä»è€Œ$\forall r\in \mathbb{Q^+}:f(rx)=rf(x)$
$1.3^\circ$ å†è¯æ˜$\forall r\in \mathbb{Q}:f(rx)=rf(x)$
ç”±äº$f(x)=f(0+x)=f(0)+f(x)$ï¼Œå› æ­¤$f(0)=0$
ä»è€Œ$f(x)+f(-x)=f(0)=0$ï¼Œå³$f(x)=-f(-x)$
ä»¤ä¸Šå¼ä¸­çš„$x=\frac{m}{n}y$ï¼Œæœ‰$f\left( -\frac{m}{n}y \right)=-f\left( \frac{m}{n}y \right)=-\frac{m}{n}f(y)$
å³è¯ï¼š$\forall r\in \mathbb{Q}:f(rx)=rf(x)$
$1.4^\circ$ å†è¯æ˜$f(x)$å¤„å¤„è¿ç»­
ä»»å–$x_{0}\in \mathbb{R}$ï¼Œå°†xå†™æˆ$x=x_{0}+\Delta x$ï¼Œå°±æœ‰ï¼š
$\begin{align}\lim_\limits{ x \to  x_0 }f(x)&=\lim_\limits{ \Delta x \to  0 }f(x_{0}+\Delta x)\\&=\lim_\limits{ \Delta x \to  0 }[f(x_{0})+f(\Delta x)]\\&=f(x_{0})+\lim_\limits{ \Delta x \to  0 }f(\Delta x)\\&=f(x_{0})\end{align}$
$1.5^\circ$ å†è¯æ˜$\forall r\in \mathbb{J}:f(rx)=rf(x)$
ç”±è¿ç»­å‡½æ•°ä¾‹é¢˜2å³å¾—
$2^\circ$ ç”±äº$\forall c\in(-\infty,+\infty):f(cx)=cf(x)$ï¼Œå› æ­¤$f(x)=f(1\cdot x)=xf(1)$ï¼Œä»¤$a=f(1)$ï¼Œå°±æœ‰$f(x)=ax$
è¯æ¯•

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 2 </span>
å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹$f(x+y)+f(x-y)=2f(x)\cdot f(y)\quad(\forall x,y\in \mathbb{R})$åœ¨å®è½´$\mathbb{R}$ä¸Šä¸æ’ä¸ºé›¶çš„è¿ç»­è§£æ˜¯$f(x)=\cos ax$æˆ–$f(x)=\mathrm{ch}\,ax$(aä¸ºå¸¸æ•°)

>[!note] 
>äº‹å®ä¸Šï¼Œæœ‰ï¼š
>$\cos x= \frac{e^{ix}+e^{-ix}}{2},\quad \mathrm{ch}\,x= \frac{e^x+e^{-x}}{2}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$1^\circ$ å…ˆè¯æ˜$f(0)=1,f(x)$ä¸ºå¶å‡½æ•°
å¯¹äº$f(x+y)+f(x-y)=2f(x)\cdot f(y)\quad(\forall x,y\in \mathbb{R})$ï¼Œ
ä»¤$y=0,$æœ‰$f(0)=1$
ä»¤$x=0,$æœ‰$f(-y)=f(y)$å³å‡½æ•°ä¸ºå¶å‡½æ•°
$2^\circ$ ç”¨æ¨å½’æ³•è¯æ˜æ±‚è§£
ç”±äº$f(0)=1,$ç”±å±€éƒ¨ä¿å·æ€§ï¼Œ$\exists c>0,s.t.\forall x\in[0,c]:f(x)>0$
åˆ†ä¸ºä¸¤ç§æƒ…å†µï¼š
(a)è‹¥$f(c)\leqslant1$ï¼Œç”±äº$0<f(c)\leqslant1$ï¼ŒçŸ¥$\exists \theta\in\left[ 0, \frac{\pi}{2} \right],s.t.f(c)=\cos \theta$
å°†æ–¹ç¨‹å†™æˆï¼š$f(x+y)=2f(x)f(y)-f(x-y)$
ä»¤$x=y=c$ï¼Œæœ‰$f(2c)=2f^2(c)-f(0)=2\cos^2 \theta-1=\cos2\theta$
ä¸‹é¢ç”¨å¼ºå½’çº³æ³•è¯æ˜$f(nc)=\cos n\theta$
å½“$n=1,2$æ—¶ï¼Œä¸Šé¢å·²ç»è¯æ˜ï¼š$f(c)=\cos \theta,f(2c)=\cos2\theta$
å‡è®¾å¯¹äº$1,2,\dots n-2,n-1$å·²æˆç«‹ï¼Œå°±æœ‰$f[(n-2)c]=\cos(n-2)\theta,f[(n-1)c]=\cos(n-1)\theta$
ä»¤$x=(n-1)c,y=c$æœ‰$f(nc)=2\cos(n-1)\theta \cos \theta-\cos(n-2)\theta=\cos n\theta$
ç”±å½’çº³æ³•åŸç†ï¼Œå°±æœ‰$\forall n\in \mathbb{N},f(nc)=\cos n\theta\quad(1)$
ä»¤$x=y=\frac{c}{2}$ï¼Œå°±æœ‰$f^2\left( \frac{c}{2} \right)=\frac{1}{2}(\cos \theta +1)=\cos^2 \frac{\theta}{2}$
åˆç”±äº$\frac{c}{2}\in[0,c]$ï¼Œäºæ˜¯$f\left( \frac{c}{2} \right)>0$ï¼Œæ•…$f\left( \frac{c}{2} \right)=\cos \frac{\theta}{2}$
ç”±å¼±å½’çº³æ³•ï¼Œè‹¥å·²æœ‰$f\left( \frac{c}{2^{n-1}} \right)=\cos \frac{\theta}{2^{n-1}}$
ä»¤$x=y=\frac{\theta}{2^n}$ï¼Œä¾¿æœ‰$f^2\left( \frac{c}{2^n} \right)=\frac{1}{2}\left( \cos \frac{\theta}{2^{n-1}} +1 \right)=\cos^2 \frac{\theta}{2^n}$
åŒç†ï¼Œ$f\left( \frac{c}{2^n} \right)=\cos \frac{\theta}{2^n}\quad(2)$
åˆ©ç”¨å¼$(1),(2)$ï¼Œå°±æœ‰$f\left( \frac{m}{2^n}c \right)=\cos\frac{m}{2^n}\theta$
ç”±äº$\left\{  \frac{p}{q} |p,q\in \mathbb{N}^+ \right\}$åœ¨æ­£çš„å®æ•°è½´ä¸Šç¨ å¯†ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥å¯¹äºä»»æ„$x>0$ï¼Œéƒ½å¯ä»¥å†™æˆ$\frac{m}{2^n}$å½¢å¼çš„å®æ•°çš„æé™
å³$\forall x>0,\exists x_{i}(i=1,2\dots)(x_{i}å½¢å¦‚\frac{m}{2^n})s.t.x_{i}\to x(i\to+\infty)$
åˆ™$f(x_{i}c)=\cos x_{i}\theta$ï¼Œç”±è¿ç»­æ€§ï¼Œ$f(xc)=\lim_\limits{ i \to \infty }f(x_{i}c)=\cos \theta x$
åˆç”±äºä¸ºå¶å‡½æ•°ä¸”$f(0)=1$ï¼Œæ•…å¯¹äº$x\in \mathbb{R}$å‡æˆç«‹
ä»¤$xc=y,è®° \frac{\theta}{c}=a$ï¼Œå°±æœ‰$f(y)=\cos ay$
(b)è‹¥$f(c)>1$ï¼Œç±»ä¼¼æ±‚è§£
è¯æ¯•

>[!note] 
>ä»¥ä¸‹ä¸¤é¢˜å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡è½¬åŒ–æ³•æ±‚è§£ï¼Œå³é€šè¿‡å˜é‡æ›¿æ¢ï¼ŒæŠŠå®ƒä»¬è½¬æ¢ä¸ºå·²è¯æ˜çš„ç»“æœ

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 3 </span>
å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹$f(x+y)=f(x)\cdot f(y)\quad(\forall x,y\in \mathbb{R})$åœ¨å®è½´$\mathbb{R}$ä¸Š**å”¯ä¸€**ä¸æ’ä¸ºé›¶çš„è¿ç»­è§£æ˜¯$f(x)=a^x$(a>0ä¸ºå¸¸æ•°)

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
$1^\circ$ è¯æ˜$f(x)>0$
ç”±äº$f(x)\not\equiv0$ï¼Œæ•…$\exists x_{0}\in \mathbb{R},f(x_{0})\neq0$
åœ¨å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹ä¸­ï¼Œä»¤$y=x_{0}-x$ï¼Œå°±æœ‰$f(x)f(x_{0}-x)=f(x_{0})\neq0$ï¼Œå°±æœ‰$f(x)\neq0$
è¿›ä¸€æ­¥ï¼Œ$f(x)=f\left( \frac{x}{2}+\frac{x}{2} \right)=f^2\left( \frac{x}{2} \right)>0$
$2^\circ$ ä½œå˜é‡ä»£æ¢
ä»¤$F(x)=\log_{a}f(x)$ï¼Œåˆæœ‰$f(1)>0$ï¼Œä¸å¦¨å–$a=f(1)$
äºæ˜¯$F(x)$è¿ç»­ï¼Œä¸”æ»¡è¶³æ–¹ç¨‹$F(x+y)=F(x)+F(y)\quad(\forall x,y\in \mathbb{R})$
ç”±ä¾‹1å¾—ï¼Œ$F(x)=a_{1}x$ï¼Œä½†$F(1)=\log_{a}a=1$ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥$a_{1}=F(1)=1$ï¼Œæ•…$F(x)=x$
ä»è€Œ$f(x)=a^{F(x)}=a^x(a=f(1)>0)$
è¯æ¯•

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 4 </span>
å‡½æ•°æ–¹ç¨‹$f(xy)=f(x)+f(y)\quad(\forall x,y>0)$**å”¯ä¸€**ä¸æ’ä¸ºé›¶çš„è¿ç»­è§£æ˜¯$f(x)=b\log_ax$(a>0,bä¸ºå¸¸æ•°)

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof ï¼š</span>
ä»¤$g(x)=f(a^x)$ï¼Œå°±æœ‰$g(x+y)=g(x)+g(y)$
åŒç†å¯å¾—
è¯æ¯•
